(According to this, the fact that the awakening of the original desire for kindness was brought about through the deeds of the lower beings [that is, the Jewish people], because of which, it arose in His thought and desire [to emanate, create form and actualize. – reaches the beginning of the arousal of desire in His essential thought etc.)
This is the meaning of the verses,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 40:6</i> “Your wonders and thoughts toward us etc. are beyond telling,” and,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 147:5</i> “His <i>Tevunah</i>-understanding is beyond calculation.”
This is because the level of depth of the essential thought in the essential Light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), is in accordance to the [infinite] depth of His insight and focus (<i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Daat</i>), as in the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 92:6</i> “How very deep are Your thoughts,” as mentioned before. This is sufficient for the understanding.
In the same manner we can understand on lower levels, such as the chaining down of the desire and thought of the simple unity after the first <i>Tzimtzum</i>, which is called the “Empty Space” etc.
For example, the aspect of the radiance of the “line” etc., is the aspect of the “Primal desire and thought,” in that He foresees everything in one glance etc. This level also has the three levels of thought, speech and action in it.
(This is called Creation-<i>Briyah</i>, Formation-<i>Yetzirah</i> and Action-<i>Asiyah</i>.<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtza’ee, Hanachot 5577 p. 202 and elsewhere.</i> Thought is in <i>Briyah</i>, speech is in <i>Yetzirah</i> and action is in <i>Asiyah</i>, as written,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 43:7</i> “I created it, I formed it and I even actualized it,” as known).
This principle continues to the desire of the hidden thought of <i>Adam Kadmon</i>, to <i>Atik Yomin</i>, to <i>Arich Anpin</i> etc., as it descends lower in the chaining down of the worlds in a manner of particulars.
This is similar to the example in man below. The radiance of the light of the essential thought hidden in the essential self of the [human] soul descends with the revelation of desire, intellect and emotions etc. until it reaches the aspect of thought, which enclothes the emotions of the heart. The thought that enclothes the emotions is called “<i>Leah</i>,” and also includes the three levels of thought, speech and action etc., as mentioned before.
Now, in regard to how it is Above, this applies until the aspect of the letters of the thoughts of His emotions in <i>Atzilut</i>, which is called <i>Zeir Anpin</i>. About this it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 8:21</i> “And <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה said (<i>VaYomer</i>-וי<b>אמר</b>) to His heart” – this “saying-<i>Amirah</i>-אמירה” is in thought etc.
Sometimes the matter remains in the supernal thought of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, which is called, “The Supernal Man,” as in,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 6:6</i> “And <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה regretted etc.” – which reverted to thought that was never brought into speech or action altogether.
This is similar to the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Midrash Tehillim 89:1</i> “The heart did not reveal it to the mouth.” It is also similar to,<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Niddah 16b</i> “Whether someone will be righteous or wicked He did not say (ק<b>אמר</b>),” as known. This is sufficient for the understanding.
(Now, in explanation of the aspect of the three levels of thought, speech and action as it relates to the general worlds; <i>Adam Kadmon</i> is in thought, which is the aspect of the, “Man of <i>Briyah</i>.” The aspect of <i>Atik Yomin</i> and <i>Arich Anpin</i> is the aspect of speech, which is the, “Man of <i>Yetzirah</i>” and the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> is called the “Man of Asiyah.”
Now more specifically, <i>Zeir Anpin</i> also includes the three levels of <i>Briyah</i>, <i>Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i> - that is, thought, speech and action, within itself.)
A person who understands the general principle from the accumulation of the particulars, will understand from the aspect of the action of the essential thought in the essence of the light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), to the aspect of the action within the thought of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>.
About this the verse states,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 135:6</i> “Everything that <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה desires” – in His essential thought – “He did” – from the “nothingness” of <i>Atzilut</i> to <i>Briyah</i> etc.)
Now, the matter of, “The big <i>Dalet</i>-ד of One-<i>Echad</i>-אח<b>ד</b>” may be understood in the same way.
It is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Tevunah</i> from behind <i>Imma</i> etc., which is the matter of the knot of the Tefillin of the head etc., as known.<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III (<i>Ra’aya Mehemna</i>) 236b; Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar HaTefillin, Shaar 4, Ch. 5; Likkutei Torah of the Arizal to Exodus 33:23.</i>
It may be understood in a manner of the particulars of the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, which is called “One-<i>Echad</i>-אחד,” being that it is the aspect of the oneness of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> (which in the aspect of the general worlds is called the “Man of Action (<i>Adam d’Asiyah</i>)”).
This is the root of the thought of <i>Leah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar HaTefillin, Shaar 8, Ch. 13.</i> which comes in an aspect of letters and combinations, and is called “Thought of Thought.”
(However, it is called, “The big <i>Dalet</i>-ד,” indicating that it is the aspect of the mature state of speech (<i>Gadloot HaDibur</i>). For, as explained above, there are two levels in this.
In truth, however, this too is considered to be, “Speech of thought,” in that He thinks the concept in combinations, even without intending to bring it into speech at all.
This is the, “Big <i>Dalet</i>-ד” of <i>Alef Chet</i>-א״ח-9 (The first two letters of One-<i>Echad</i>-אחד) which are the nine sefirot<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">The letters <i>Alef-Chet</i>-א״ח have a numerical value of nine.</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar HaTefillin, Shaar 8, Ch. 12.</i> That is, every emotion and <i>Sefirah</i> comes in the letters and combinations of the thought of <i>Leah</i> etc., from the power and root of thought, which is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Tevunah</i> etc.
It is because of this that one must elongate the <i>Dalet</i>-ד [when reciting the <i>Shema</i>].<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Brachot 13b</i> This is because it is the root of the aspect of Kingship-<i>Malchut</i> within the four directions of the world in the lower unity of,<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 18b; Talmud Bavli, Pesachim 56a</i> “Blessed is the name of His glorious kingdom forever and ever etc.)
Now, one may also understand this in a general way, in regard to the “Primal thought” up to the Simple thought in His Simple Unity, literally in the Essential Self of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה Himself, blessed is He, in the aspect of “The Concealed of all concealed”<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Introduction to Zohar 2a</i> that no thought can grasp,<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Introduction to Tikkunei Zohar 17a</i> even the thought of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> etc., this being that the big <i>Dalet</i>-ד is when it arose in the letters of His simple thought and desire etc., which comes from His Essential <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Tevunah</i>. This is sufficient for those of understanding.
(As to what is written in Etz Chayim, that “the heels of <i>Leah</i> enter the head of <i>Rachel</i> etc.,” and similarly, in regards to what the sages stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, (<i>Shaar Leah V’Rachel</i>) Shaar 38, Ch. 3; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza’ee, Vayikra Vol. 1, p. 253; Torat Chayim, Vayeitze 173c, note 20.</i> “That which humility made the heel of her soles, fear of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה made the crown of her head etc.,” this refers to the aspect of speech of thought that becomes thought of speech. This is the meaning of the “Heel of humility.”
This is because thought is in a state of concealment and nothingness, whereas speech is in a state of revelation and somethingness etc., and thought (<i>Machshavah</i>) becomes the crown of <i>Rachel</i>, which is the aspect of speech (<i>Dibur</i>).
This is because the aspect of the power, root and beginning of speech are the combinations of the letters of thought. For, if the combinations of thought cease, so does speech cease, as known.
This is the meaning of<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 22:4</i> “The heel of humility is the fear of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה etc.,” as explained elsewhere.)

Chapter 44

We may now also understand the root of the matter of the division of the letters of thought from the aspect of the five severities (<i>MaNTzePa”Ch)</i> etc., [as they apply] much higher<i>,</i> even in the “Essential Thought” [before <i>Tzimtzum</i>] and the “Primordial Thought” [after <i>Tzimtzum</i>] (<i>Machshavah HaKedooma)</i> and the “Hidden Thought” (<i>Machshavah Stima’ah)</i> of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> and <i>Arich Anpin</i>, until the thought of <i>Zeir Anpin,</i> in the way explained before in detail about man below; that the root of the letter-divisions of the combinations come from higher than the source of the comprehension of <i>Binah</i> itself etc.
This is the matter of <i>Ma'amar Satoom</i> – “The Closed Saying,” and <i>Ma'amar Patu'ach</i> – “The Open Saying.”<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Shabbat 104a; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Shemot Vol.1 p. 213; Shaarei Teshuva 91b.</i>
An example is the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:3</i> “And God said-<i>VaYomer Elohi”m</i>-ויאמר אלהי״ם.” <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם represents the one hundred and twenty combinations<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 15, Ch. 6; Shaar 44, Ch. 5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Shemot Vol. 1, p.137 – There are 120 possible permutations of the five letters of <i>HaShem</i>’s-יהו״ה primary title God-<i>Elohi”m</i>-<i>אלהי״ם.</i></i> of the “Hidden Thought” that is literally in the Essential Self. This is called, “The closed saying” that is concealed within the Essential Self of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, He who is called the “Concealed of all concealments etc.,” to the highest heights, as in the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Job 28:23</i> “And <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם understands the way thereof etc.”
This aspect of <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם is the aspect of the “constraint and withdrawal” (<i>Tzimtzum v’Histalkut)</i>. This is as stated by our sages,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">See Rashi to Genesis 1:1; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiyot HaTorah Vol. 1 pg. 337; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 4, p. 1,420.</i> “At first it arose in thought to create through the quality of judgment,” which is the name <i>Elohim-</i>אלהי״ם etc.
That is, this also refers to the aspect of the letter-divisions of the combinations of the, “Hidden Thought” (<i>Machshava Stima’ah)</i>.
(This accords with the translation of Onkelos<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">See Onkelos translation to Genesis 1:1</i> on the word “<i>Bereishit</i>-in the beginning, as being <i>B'Kadmin-</i>בקדמין, which refers to the Primal Desire (<i>Ratzon HaKadoom-</i>רצון הקדום), that is, the “Desire of the Primordial Thought” (<i>Machshavah HaKedooma</i>-מחשבה הקדומה), which is called the aspect of <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם in an aspect of constraint and division, according to the statement of our sages that,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Rosh HaShanah 32a</i> “<i>Bereishit</i> is also a [creative] utterance (<i>Maamar)</i>”; in that it is the aspect of the Hidden Saying (<i>Ma'amar Satoom</i>) of the Hidden Thought (<i>Machshava HaStoomah</i>), until the aspect of the Simple Essential Thought, as discussed before.
As known, <i>Elohi”m</i>-אלהים consists of the letters<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar, Introduction 2a; Also see <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch</i> p. 472</i> “<i>Mi Eileh</i>-מי אלה,” which is the aspect of the division [of letters], as in [the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 40:26</i> “lift your gaze heavenwards and see] Who-<i>Mi-</i>מי created These-<i>Eileh</i>-אלה.”
Now, the upper <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם is the <i>Binah</i> and hidden thought of <i>Arich Anpin</i> and <i>Adam Kadmon</i>, while the lower <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Tevunah</i> and <i>Leah</i> etc.
This is as stated in the <i>Zohar</i><sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Tikkunei Zohar 112c; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Vayikra Vol. 2, p. 625; Devarim Vol. 2, p. 651; Drushei Chatuna Vol. 1, p. 45; Torat Chayim, Noach p. 46c.</i> that the thirty-two [times that is says] “And God said-<i>VaYomer Elohi”m</i>-ויאמר אלהי״ם” [in the account of creation,]<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1</i> refer to the thirty-two pathways<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar III (<i>Idra Rabba</i>) 128b; 129a; 136a; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 1, The Gate of His Title (<i>Shaar HaKinuy</i>).</i> that open up in <i>Binah</i>.
All these are the aspect of the hidden, “Closed Saying” (<i>Maamar Satoom</i>) of speech of thought, from which the thought of the speech of <i>Malchut,</i> which is called the “Open Saying” is made, as will be explained on the subject of the aspect of the Closed letter <i>Mem</i>-ם and the open letter <i>Mem</i>-מ etc.)
However, in regard to the root of this power of division; although it comes in an aspect of constraint (<i>Tzimtzum</i>), nonetheless, it is from higher than the power and source of the comprehension itself etc.
This is as stated in the Zohar regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Song of Songs 2:12; Zohar I 97b; Also see Sefer HaMaamarim 5568 Vol.1, p. 488.</i> “And the voice of the turtledove (<i>Tor</i>-תור) is heard in our land etc.” That is, this refers to the aspect of the voice of <i>Binah</i> that is heard in an aspect of divisions of combinations by means of the five severities <i>MaNTzePa”Ch</i> (מנצפ״ך) etc., which is when the illumination comes into an aspect of speech, this being the revealed world that is called, “our land-<i>Artzeinu</i>-ארצנו” etc.
This is as explained above at length from the analogy of an infant, that he does not have thought in divisions of letters until he speaks etc.
For as soon as there is the power to combine in speech from <i>Chochmah</i>, that is, from the inner aspect of <i>Chochmah</i>; then there is a power to combine the letters of thought from the innerness and source of <i>Binah</i> etc.
However, the power that makes the combinations is specifically from the aspect of the source of <i>Binah</i>, but the combinations themselves in their particular forms, specifically follow the intent of the specific comprehension, according to the constraint of the thought of the “Analytical Intellect” (<i>Sechel HaIyunit)</i> that gives order to the manner of the combinations etc., as discussed before.
In truth, this is an aspect of the Open <i>Mem</i>-מ. This is because in <i>Binah</i> itself there is a closed <i>Mem</i>-ם and an open <i>Mem</i>-מ,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">See Pardes Rimonim, Shaar 27, Ch. 16.</i> which are called <i>Maamar Satoom</i> (a Closed [hidden] Saying), and <i>Maamar Patuach</i> (an Open [revealed] Saying).
For, every <i>Maamar</i> (Saying) is within the thought of <i>Binah</i> itself.
This is [the explanation of] the matter of the difference between the encompassing lights of <i>Imma</i>, which are still in an aspect of the “Closed <i>Mem”</i> (ם) that encompasses from all sides and specifically is square, as stated in the <i>Zohar</i><sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar <i>Terumah</i> 127a; Also see <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Dvarim</i> Vol.4 p. 1,228; <i>Torat Chayim, Noach</i> 57b.</i> regarding the <i>Mem</i> (ם) of the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 9:6</i> “ל<b>ם</b>רבה המשרה” – “To increase authority,” as explained elsewhere; compared to the aspect of the illumination of this encompassing light to make the divisions of combinations through the aspect of the five severities <i>MaNTzePa”Ch</i> etc.; which is the matter of the “Open <i>Mem”</i> (מ), that is, the “Open [revealed] <i>Maamar”</i> (Saying).
That is, the closed [hidden] thought becomes opened through the divisions of letters, as indicated by the form of the open <i>Mem</i>-מ, as known.
Now, the explanation of the matter is as known regarding the explanation of the encompassing lights of <i>Binah</i>, in regard to the matter of<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 22:6</i> “The mother crouches over the chicks” etc.
That is, the emotions only receive from the aspect of the comprehension of the inner light of <i>Binah</i>, which is called, “<i>Em HaBanim</i>” (The mother of the children).<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 219a; Zohar II 84a-85b; Imrei Binah, Shaar HaTefilin 99d; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch pg. 312.</i> It is then that [the emotions] are called “chicks” etc., and the aspect of the maturation of the intellect of the emotions comes in a concealed manner from the aspect of the encompassing lights, that is, when “The mother crouches over the chicks” etc. This is in order to draw that which is above the intellect of <i>Binah</i> into the emotions.
(This is similar to love that is dependent on something.<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Mishna Avot 5:16; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,498; Ateret Rosh, Shaar Yom HaKipurim pg. 68.</i>
This something comes to be loved in an aspect of an inner illumination. Therefore, when the thing is nullified, the love is nullified.
Nevertheless, [the love] remains in an aspect of an encompassing light, which is the aspect of concealment from that thing. It can therefore return to be aroused and once more come in an aspect of an inner illumination, as known.)
For it hovers over them [the emotions], and is square, in that it actually “sits” directly upon them, as explained elsewhere regarding the <i>Mem</i>-ם of “To increase<i>-LeMarbeh-</i>ל<b>ם</b>רבה” etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">See note above.</i>
The general matter can be compared by example to how the knowledge of the mind encompasses whatever it knows. For although the thing known is a separate thing, nevertheless, this knowledge surrounds and encompasses the thing on every side.
(This is like the Godly knowledge, in that He supervises and knows all creatures; in that He encompasses them with this knowledge, as explained in Tanya<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Tanya, Ch. 48, and elsewhere.</i> that, “With the knowledge of knowing the whole earth [He encompasses it] etc.)
This is similar to what it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 1:22</i> “And over the heads of the <i>Chayot</i> [angels] there was a firmament similar to ice etc.,” which also refers to the aspect of the encompassing light of <i>Binah</i> (from which the garment of the <i>Chashmal</i> is made, that is, from the aspect of the externality of <i>Binah</i>, as will be explained).
This is also explained elsewhere regarding the matter of <i>Ohr</i> (Light), <i>Mayim</i> (Water), <i>Rakia</i> (Firmament), that the comprehension of <i>Binah</i> is called “<i>Rakia</i> (Firmament).”<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">See Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shacharit 70a; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee Vayikra Vol.2, p. 451 and 472.</i>
This is because before the concept comes to be fully grasped, it still transcends the aspect of limitation in letters, such as the explanation of a deep concept that has yet to come into a limited form in the mind to be considered, grasped and comprehended.
This is called “Flowing Waters” (<i>Mayim D’Naidee</i>),<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, <i>Eruvin</i> 46a</i> in that it can come in many different manners etc.
This is not the case, however, when the concept comes in a limited manner that literally is grasped and comprehended in the organ (vessel) of his brain. It then it is compared to ice,<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 77a</i> in which “the waters have congealed and remain as they are” (<i>D’Aglidee Maya v’Kayama</i>)<i>.</i>
[The term “grasped-<i>Hasagah</i>-השגה”] is of the same terminology as<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Erechin 17a (in the Mishnah)</i> “grasped by the hand-<i>Heseg Yad-</i>השג יד” [meaning, acquired] etc. As explained elsewhere, this is called “The Firmament” (<i>Rakiya</i>), which is the matter of the ice (<i>Kerach</i>-קרח) that is upon the intellect of the <i>Chayot</i> [angels] etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch</i> p. 285</i>
However, the root of this ice, which specifically comes in an aspect that is completely concrete, is from higher than the aspect of the inner light of <i>Binah</i>.
Rather, it is drawn and made from the aspect of the encompassing light of <i>Binah</i>, which is called the closed <i>Mem</i> (ם) that altogether does not illuminate nor is drawn down into the emotions in a revealed manner.
Therefore, it is from there that an aspect of a “firmament” (<i>Rakiya-</i>רקיע) or “ice” (<i>Kerach</i>-קרח) is made upon the intellect of the emotions etc.
This then [is the meaning of], “And the mother crouches etc.,” and similarly,<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 32:11</i> “He hovers over his young etc.,” which is the aspect of the garment of the <i>Chashmal</i> (חשמ״ל) that encompasses [the emotions] as a protector.
(This will be explained shortly regarding the matter of the, “Cloaks of Leather” etc., that encompass <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> (<i>Malchut</i>), until below the feet of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> (<i>Malchut</i>),<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 42, Ch. 13; Also see Torat Chayim, Noach p. 58a.</i> from which the veil that separates between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i> is made etc.)
This then, is the aspect of the source of <i>Binah</i> from which the power that makes the divisions of combinations of the letters of thought is drawn.
It is called, “The Combiner” (<i>Metzaref</i>), as opposed to the combinations themselves, which specifically are in an aspect of the, “Open <i>Mem”</i> (מ) and the “Open Saying” (<i>Maamar Patuach)</i> etc. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 45

Now it is written,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 3:21; Also see Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shacharit 60d; Birchat HaMazon 115b; Milah 147a-148d; Biurei Zohar, Balak 149d; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Vayikra Vol. 2, pg. 493; Torah Or, Lech Lecha 12c.</i> “And <i>HaShem Elohim-</i>יהו"ה אלהי"ם made for Adam and his wife cloaks of leather (<i>Ohr-</i><b>ע</b>ור) and garbed them.”
This refers to the aspect of the <i>Chashmal</i> of <i>Nogah</i> that encompasses <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah (Malchut)</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>, who are called Adam and his wife, [which encompasses them] until below their feet, as known.
Now, in the Torah scroll of Rabbi Meir<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">See Midrash Bereishit Raba 20:12; Shaar HaEmunah 43a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit pg. 450; Bamidbar Vol. 2, pg. 560 &amp; p. 757; Devarim Vol. 1, pg. 115; Drushei Chatunah Vol. 1, pg. 66; Hanachot 5577 pg. 253.</i> this was written with an <i>Aleph</i>-א, that is, “Light-<i>Ohr-</i><b>א</b>ור.”
This refers to the upper radiance<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 36b – <i>Zihara Ila’ah</i></i> about which it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 104:2</i> “He covers Himself with light as a garment,” this being after the rectification of the two-hundred and eighty-eight [sparks] etc.
Now, we must first have some understanding into the explanation of the matter of the shattering and rectification [of the vessels] in general.
This [took place] in the aspect of the letters (<i>Otiyot</i>-אותיות), which are called vessels (<i>Keilim</i>).<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Tanya, Shaar HaYichud V'HaEmunah Ch. 4 and elsewhere.</i>
They shattered and fell because of the overabundance of light which they were incapable of containing, as stated in <i>Etz Chayim</i>.<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 10, Ch. 5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,476.</i>
This is like the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 74:13</i> “You caused the sea (<i>Yam-</i>ים) to fracture with Your might.”<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">The term “sea-<i>Yam</i>-ים” refers to <i>Malchut</i>, which is the letters, as it states (Ecclesiastes 1:7), “All the streams flow into the sea (<i>HaYam</i>-הים). See Shaarei Orah of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla translated as Gates of Light, Shaar 1 (<i>Malchut</i>); Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One.</i>
This refers to the aspect of <i>Tohu</i> (Chaos),<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch pg. 5; Torat Chayim, Vayeishev 206c.</i> wherein the aspect of the letters fragmented, this being called, “The Shattering of the Vessels” (<i>Shvirat HaKelim</i>), as known.
The reason for this, as known, is analogous to a deep conceptual light that transcends the limitations of the organ (vessel) of the brain [to contain]. The letters of the thought of the concept will certainly become confused, because of their inability to contain the light, since it is too great for them.
The opposite is true when the organ (vessel) of the brain is able to contain the light of the deep concept. On the contrary, it becomes limited, settled and concealed within these letters (that is, it is absorbed).
However, when they are incapable of containment, then of necessity, the letters become fragmented.
It is as explained elsewhere at length,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch pg. 5 and on; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Nevi'im pg. 5 and on.</i> that this is like when a word falls short of containing the great light [of meaning] that is within it; its letters scatter here and there, until nothing at all can be understood from them.
An example is the word “And He said-<i>Vayomer-</i>ויאמר.” When it cannot contain the depth of its intended [meaning], its letters scatter and all that remains is its <i>Vav</i>-ו and <i>Mem</i>-מ, out of order and displaced.
(This is similar to the letters of the fleeting thoughts of the heart during the day. They become disjointed, displaced and out of order when one dreams [at night].<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Brachot 55b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Hanachot 5577 p. 244</i>
They come about from the combinations of thoughts one thinks during the day, but out of order. Rather, [they come in a jumble], one letter from this word and another letter from that word etc.
It thus states,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Zacharia 10:2</i> “dreams speak nonsense etc.,” as explained elsewhere.<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Torat Chayim, VaYechi 245d</i>)
This fragmentation is called a “Shattering” (<i>Shvirah)</i> into many small parts.
This is because when a letter that separated unto itself comes elsewhere, it only contains an exceedingly diminished portion of the full concept, as the word was in its complete form etc.
Moreover, it too undergoes one fragmentation after another, until it becomes completely alienated from its [original] meaning.
(This may be compared to the matter of dreams that come from the thoughts of one’s heart during the day. However, one cannot dream of,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, <i>Brachot</i> 55b; <i>Torat Chayim, VaYetze</i> 169d; <i>Miketz</i> 216a</i> “An elephant going through the eye of a needle,” but rather only reflections of the thoughts of his heart [during the day], as discussed elsewhere regarding Joseph’s interpretation of dreams,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Inyanim</i> p. 431; <i>Torat Chayim, VaYechi</i> p. 245c &amp; 248c.</i> and as will be explained later.)
Likewise, we may understand how it is supernally, in regard to the matter of the shattering of the vessels of the lights of <i>Tohu</i> (Chaos), that it is an aspect of the fragmentation and scattering of their letters, as stated, “You scattered [the sea (<i>Yam</i>-ים)] etc.”
This is to say that they fell lower and lower until they came into an aspect of being an “alien garment.”
This is the root of the matter of the coming into being of the aspect of the garment of the <i>Chashmal</i> etc., which is called garments of skin (<i>Or-</i><b>ע</b>ור).
Now, as known, these “Skins” are the aspect of the three kinds of letters; thought, speech and action,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">See Biurei HaZohar, VaYeshev 21d; Tazriah 73b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 923; Na”Ch pg. 318; Kuntreisim pg. 209</i> which are rooted in the letters of the vessels of <i>Tohu</i> (Chaos) that fragmented and fell down, thus making the aspect of an encompassing garment to garb the aspect of the emotions of man etc.
Although it became an aspect of a separate garment, its root is from above the source of the intellect of <i>Binah</i> as it is in the emotions.
This also is the aspect of the externality of <i>Binah</i> that, “hovers over the chicks,” to protect them etc., which is from the aspect of the encompassing light of <i>Binah</i>, in the aspect of the previously discussed closed <i>Mem</i>-ם. This will suffice for the understanding.
Now, to understand this with additional explanation, it is known that this is also the root of the matter of analogies, such as the three hundred analogies of Rabbi Meir etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Sanhedrin 38b</i> in that the root of the analogy is higher than the analogue,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">See Sefer HaMaamarim 5568 Vol. 1, pg. 393; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Vayikra Vol. 2, pg. 522 and on.</i> as are the analogies [proverbs] of Solomon, which are exceedingly deep [concepts of] wisdom.
They thus do not have an aspect of “vessels of letters,” except through being enclothed in matters that are very separate from the essential wisdom. It is specifically there, [in the analogy,] that the depth of the wisdom may be grasped, just as one grasps the depth of a concept.
This may only be [accomplished] specifically through analogy, for it cannot be grasped even with abundant explanations etc.
Moreover, for an analogy to be made specifically according to the analogue, of necessity it must reach the depth and source from which the analogue comes out. If not, the analogy will not at all be in line with the analogue, as known.
This being the case, the root of the analogy is in the source concept of the analogue, and higher than it.
For this reason, it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 1:6</i> “The words of the wise and their riddles”; that commensurate to the depth and source of the wisdom, so will be the depth of the riddles and analogies, such as the analogies of Rabbi Meir and the analogies of Solomon.
This is explained elsewhere regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Kings I 5:12</i> “And he spoke three thousand proverbs;” that is, [each analogy was] an analogy for [the previous] analogy, as explained in the Zohar that the very last analogy contains the very first depth and source of the analogue etc.
The same holds true of the root of the aspect of letters. It is specifically through them that the light of the intellect is grasped well etc.
(This may similarly be understood regarding the light of the intellect becoming concrete. To the degree that it comes to be concretely grasped and explained on the lowest level, it is specifically there that the aspect of the depth and inner light of the intellect itself is [grasped] etc.)
The [above] is also the case with the aspect of the externality of <i>Binah</i> from which the aspect of the <i>Chashmal</i> garment of <i>Binah</i> is made.<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">See Or HaTorah, Noach Vol. 3, pg. 1338</i>
It is regarding this that it states, “And he made cloaks of skin-<i>Or</i>-<b>ע</b>ור etc.,” which is the aspect of the protector of the intellect within the emotions, so as not to come to an aspect of error.
(It is from this that the placenta for the fetus is made etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">As will be explained later regarding the development of <i>Klipah</i>.</i>)
This is as explained at length elsewhere<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee VaYikra Vol. 2, pg. 494.</i> regarding the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III (<i>Ra'aya Mehemna</i>) 256a; Torat Chayim, Vayetze 170c; Biurei HaZohar, Noach 4c and on.</i> “The mother spreads her wings etc.,” and regarding the matter of “<i>baShalom</i>-בשלום-in peace,” which is the same letters as “<i>Malbush</i>-מלבוש-garment” etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">See Siddur of the <i>Arizal</i>, end of <i>Amida</i>; Also see Emek HaMelech, Shaar 1, Ch. 55 (9c); Torat Chayim, Noach 58a.</i> and regarding the matter of the <i>Sechach</i> (covering) of the <i>Sukkah</i> and the like.<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">See Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shaar HaSukkot p. 257a and on.</i> This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 46

However, as mentioned above, in the Torah of Rabbi Meir it was written, “Cloaks of light-<i>Katnot Ohr</i>-כתנות <b>א</b>ור,” with an <i>Aleph</i>-א etc.
For as known, the aspect of <i>Tikkun</i>-Rectification is from the aspect of the <i>Shem Ma”H HaChadash</i> – the new name of <i>Ma”H</i>-מ”ה-45 [יו״ד ה״א וא״ו ה״א] of <i>Adam Kadmon</i>, and as discussed elsewhere, this is the aspect of the eighth king, which is the root of the rectification of <i>Ma”H</i>-מ”ה of <i>Chochmah</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim (<i>Shaar HaTikun</i>), Shaar 10, Ch. 2 &amp; Ch. 3; Also see Torah Or, VaYechi 103b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,482.</i>
(This is the aspect of <i>Yosef</i> who is the interpreter of dreams.<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">See Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 1 and on. Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 4, p. 1,376. Torat Chayim VaYishlach p. 188d; VaYechi 243d; Torat Levi Yitzchak, Taanit p. 11.</i>
For the exile is compared to a dream state,<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">See Torah Or, Vayeshev 28c; Torat Chayim, Shemot, pg. 52.</i> and it resembles the thoughts of the heart of <i>Zeir Anpin,</i> which is in an aspect of sleep that is called the <i>Durmita</i>-Slumber and the withdrawal of the intellect etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 29, Ch. 1; Mevo She'arim, Shaar 3, part 2, Ch. 17; Torat Chayim Shemot pg. 53b.</i>
And from the letters of the imaginations of the dreams he combines them into good, rectified combinations, according to the source of the depth of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> that is in the forehead etc.
This is why <i>Tofer-</i>תופר-tailor shares the same letters as <i>Porat</i>-פורת-fruitful<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">See Torah Or, Vayeshev pg. 29a; Likkutei Torah, Korach, pg. 55a; Torat Chayim, Vayechi, p. 242d.</i> and <i>Poter</i>-פותר-solver etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">See Agadat Bereishit Ch. 82</i> and it is for this reason that he is called <i>Avrech-</i>אברך,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 41:43; Also see Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shaar Chanukah 280c; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Devarim Vol. 1, p. 30; Bereishit p. 490.</i> as explained elsewhere at length.)
In other words, it is called a “garment of light-<i>Ohr</i>-<b>א</b>ור” with an <i>Aleph</i>-א after the rectification of the two-hundred and eighty-eight sparks that fell along with the scattering and fragmentation of the letters and vessels of <i>Tohu</i>, as we previously explained about the constricted intellect of the separated letters.
The explanation of the matter is as known, that the “garment of skins-<i>Katnot Or</i>-כתנות <b>ע</b>ור” that garb [<i>Zeir Anpin</i>] and is called the <i>Chashmal</i>, comes specifically in a way of coarseness, just like how an analogy [is coarse] relative to the analogue.
(This is also like the coarsening of an intellectual concept through many explanations until a small child can grasp it etc.)
This is the aspect of <i>Nogah</i>-luminescence, which is like a light that illuminates within the darkness, wherein its light is more recognizable, to the point that its light is more apparent and glaring than light that radiates in a bright place, as our sages stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chulin 60b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Hanachot 5577 p. 261</i> “A candle in the sunlight is ineffectual.”
In contrast, the light of a candle in thick darkness is much more glaring. This is specifically because it illuminates the thick darkness.
For, it cannot be said that, in and of itself, the light of the candle<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Shulchan Aruch Alter Rebbe, <i>Hilchot Pesach</i> 433:6</i> is essentially more luminescent in the darkness of night than in the day. Rather, it is only because darkness is its opposite that its light becomes more apparent.
This is not true radiance, in and of itself. It only appears more radiant to the eye specifically because in the darkness its light is more apparent, but only in the eye of the beholder.
This is similar to the radiance and glimmer of a precious stone when it is displayed on coarse material. It will appear to be more radiant than if it were to be displayed on clear, luminescent material, for the same reason.
(This is also like the understanding and comprehension of a deep intellectual light through an extraneous analogy, which is coarse and foreign [to the concept]. It is because of the same reason etc.)
This then, is the aspect of <i>Nogah,</i> which has two explanations, as known.
The first is like the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Job 22:28</i> “A light will shine (<i>Nogah Or</i>-נוגה אור),” or [the verse],<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Samuel II 22:29; Psalms 18:29</i> “illuminate my darkness (<i>Yagiah Chashkhi-</i>יגיה חשכי),” and the like.
The second is a term of outward protrusion.<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">See Shaarei Teshuvah 63a</i> This is like the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Samuel II 20:13</i> “When he veered (<i>Hogah-</i>הגה) from the path etc.” and likewise,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Sanhedrin 90a</i> “One who pronounces (<i>HaHogeh-</i>ההוגה) the Divine Name etc.” It also is like the contemplation (<i>Higayon-</i>הגיון) of the thought, as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Joshua 1:8</i> “And you shall contemplate it (<i>V'Higita bo-</i>והגית בו) etc.” or,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 19:15</i> “The contemplation of my heart (<i>Hegyon leebee-</i>הגיון לבי) etc.”
Both these [explanations] amount to the same intended meaning.<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">See Imrei Binah, Shaar HaTefilin 97d.</i>
This was explained elsewhere, by way of example, from the light of the sun<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">See Imrei Binah, Shaar HaTefilin 97d; Maamarei Admor HaZaken al Maamarei RaZa”L, p. 479; Maamarei Admor HaEmtza'ee, Na”Ch p. 350.</i> as it radiates through a cloud; that its light is increased there and is more recognizable than [when looking at the light that comes from] the body of the sun itself.
For, because of the refined physicality of the cloud and the composition of the element of water in it, the details of the light are more recognizable there.
This is like the three primary colors of the rainbow, which is also called, “the appearance of the <i>Nogah-</i>הנוגה<i>,</i>” as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 1:28</i> “Like the appearance of a rainbow etc. so was the appearance of the <i>Nogah-</i>brightness.”
This is like how the specific elements and colors of a precious stone are not so recognizable except when it is set in a setting, but not in a coarse setting, but rather in a bright and shiny setting that causes its light to radiate more.
So likewise, is the matter of the second meaning of <i>Nogah</i>, in that it is an aspect of the protrusion in a refined substance, that has become somewhat more refined. There the light stands out and radiates, as in the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 18:29</i> “[<i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, my God[ illuminate my darkness (<i>Yegiah Chashchi</i>-יגיה חשכי),” specifically.
This is also like the contemplation-<i>Higayon-</i>הגיון of the analytical thought (<i>Machshavah Iyunit</i>), through which the light of the intellect comes to protrude outward into the substance of the letters of contemplative thought. It is specifically then that the grasp and radiance of the depth of the concept becomes more recognized.
It is regarding this that the verse states, “And you shall contemplate it (<i>VeHigitah bo-</i>והגית בו) etc.”
This likewise is similar to the matter of analogies, through which the light of the concept stands out and is more [easily] grasped, as discussed above.
This then, is the aspect of the <i>Nogah</i> of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> in general, that is, it is the aspect of their substance that is noticeable and protrudes.
(This is as explained elsewhere regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 26:12; See Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Maamrei RaZa”L p. 216; 5566 p. 91; Derech Mitzvotecha p. 62; Likutei Torah, Acharei 31d; Chukat 66c; Hemshech 5672 Vol.1 p. 177 &amp; p. 292.</i> “Have you seen a man, who wise in his own eyes etc.” and like the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 22:24; See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 4, p. 1,493; Torat Chayim, Noach 51a; Ohr HaTorah, Noach Vol. 3, p. 1202<i>;</i> Mevo She'arim, Shaar 6 Ch. 2 &amp; Ch. 5.</i> “And his concubine whose name was Reumah-ראומה,” that is, see-<i>Re'u</i>-ראו that I am nullified (<i>Mah-</i>מה) etc., or like ecstasy into Godliness that comes in a felt way etc.)
All this is the root of the aspect of the <i>Chashmal,</i> which is made from the externality of <i>Binah</i>.
(From here the aspect of “The Wings” are made,<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar III (<i>Balak</i>) 204b; Biurei HaZohar Balak 109b.</i> as stated regarding the verse “He hovers over his young etc.,” that “the mother (<i>Imma</i>) spreads her wings etc.” It is likewise called<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Shabbat 31a</i> “The <i>Kanfei HaShechinah</i>-The <b>wings</b> of the Indwelling Presence of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה<i>,”</i> which is the root of the souls of converts etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar, Introduction 13b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577, p. 10</i>
This is also the explanation of the statement in Zohar on the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar Balak 204b; Biurei HaZohar Balak 109b.</i> “In the morning I will order (the letters of my prayer) and I will see,” [about which the Zohar comments,] “David prepared this canopy to cover over the morning of Yosef etc., he made a light to enrobe etc., until those that are called the upper wings etc.” as explained elsewhere.)
Until from this [<i>Chashmal</i>] chains down and descends even further to become an aspect of an actual <i>Masach</i>-screen that is called a “separator” which stops and separates between the [worlds of] <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i> etc., whereas the [<i>Sefirah</i>] of <i>Malchut</i> penetrates this screen (as will be explained).
However, the matter of the “garment of light-<i>Katnot Ohr</i>-כתנות <b>א</b>ור,” with an <i>Aleph</i>-א, is after the rectification and clarification of the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of the <i>Chashmal</i>.
This is by means of the essential sublimation of the new <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה (יו״ד ה״א וא״ו ה״א) of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> etc., which is the source of the aforementioned rectification, until the <i>Yesh</i>-somethingness of <i>Nogah,</i> that is noticeably felt, becomes transformed to an aspect of actual nullification to the Godly <i>Ein</i>-nothingness.
When the somethingness (<i>Yesh</i>) becomes an aspect of nothingness (<i>Ein</i>) then it is even loftier than the aspect of the nothingness of the <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה of <i>Chochmah-</i>חכ<b>מה</b> that rectifies it etc., as explained elsewhere.<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">See Likkutei Torah, Bechukotai 47b; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, p. 576.</i>
It therefore is called a “garment of light” as in the verse, “He covers Himself with light, like a garment.”
This refers to the aspect of the light of Torah after the clarification of <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה (יו״ד ה״א וא״ו ה״א) of the supernal <i>Chochmah-</i>חכ<b>מה</b> that rectifies the aspect of <i>Ba”N-</i>ב״ן (יו״ד ה״ה ו״ו ה״ה) of <i>Nogah,</i> which then ascends to be higher than the aspect of <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה.<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 5, Ch. 1; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, p. 5; Vol 2. p. 573; Vol 4. p. 1,213.</i>
(As known, the shattering was in<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 8, Ch. 1; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, p. 5.</i> <i>Sa”G-</i>ס”ג which is “coarse<i>-Gas-</i>גס,”<sup class="footnote-marker">30</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shmot Vol 2, p. 566; Devarim Vol. 2 p. 379; Torat Chayim, Bereishit 9a.</i> but after the rectification of <i>Ba”N-</i>ב״ן<i>,</i> which [is what] fell during the shattering of the vessels, it ascends back to its source in <i>Sa”G-</i>ס״ג<i>,</i><sup class="footnote-marker">31</sup><i class="footnote">See Likkutei Torah, Bechukotai 47c; Torat Chayim, Bereishit 16c.</i> which is higher than the name of <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">32</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 5, Ch. 1; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, p. 5.</i>)
This is called <i>Zihara Ila'ah</i>-The Upper Radiance, and is comparable to a very refined light within a refined and very radiant garment, through which one can gaze [and behold] a greater illumination and radiance with the eyes.
This is the opposite of the matter of <i>Nogah</i> prior to its rectification, when it is in darkness, so that it is only because of the light that radiates within the darkness that it appears to radiate brightly etc.
In contrast, the radiance of the light due to the essence of the light, when the garment itself is made of radiant and luminous light, is like radiant and clear glass, which is called,<sup class="footnote-marker">33</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar I 65b-61a and elsewhere.</i> “<i>Aspaklaria D'Nahara</i> - A lens that shines,” etc.
It is likewise called the upper radiance (<i>Zihara Ila’ah</i>) by means of which the souls gaze upon the ray of the Indwelling Presence of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה (the <i>Shechinah</i>) in the Garden of Eden etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">34</sup><i class="footnote">See Shaarei Teshuvah pg. 58c. and elsewhere.</i> as discussed elsewhere. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 47

We now must understand the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> which is called <i>Olam HaDibbur</i>-The World of Speech,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar I 86b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, pg. 382</i> the aspect of <i>Rachel</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 4, Ch. 1; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol .1 p. 227.</i> <i>Alma D'Itgalia</i>-the Revealed World, and <i>Imma Tata'a</i>-The Lower Mother.<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Tanya Ch. 52</i> It is the final <i>Heh</i>-ה of the Name <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה.<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Zohar Vayikra</i> 17a; <i>Torat Chayim, VaYetze</i> 167c.</i>
(As known regarding the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 16:44</i> “Like mother like daughter,” that the upper <i>Heh</i>-ה of <i>Binah</i> lends the five <i>Gevurot MeNaTzePa”Ch</i> (מנצפ״ך) to the daughter, which is the aspect of the five organs of speech in the mouth, as mentioned previously.)
It is also called the <i>Maamar Patuach</i>-The Open Saying, as in,<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:3</i> “And God said-<i>Vayomer Elohi”m</i>-ויאמר אלהי״ם” or as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 33:6</i> “By the word of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה the heavens [were made] etc.” regarding which it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 103:19</i> “His Kingship rules over all etc.” as known.
For as known regarding the matter of the <i>Nesirah</i>-Separation, that at first they were two (ד”ו) <i>Partzufim-</i>statures in one,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar 24, Ch. 1 &amp; 2</i> that is, the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> was included in the aspect of the back of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>. This is as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 2:23</i> “Bone of my bones [and flesh of my flesh; she shall be called woman (אשה)] because she was taken from man (איש) etc.”
However, after the <i>Nesirah</i>-Separation, <i>Malchut</i> was built into an independent <i>Partzuf</i>-stature with lights and vessels, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 2:22</i> “And <i>HaShem Elohi”m-</i>יהו"ה אלהי"ם built the side [that He had taken from man] etc.”
The explanation of the matter is as known from various places in Zohar and Etz Chayim, that <i>Malchut</i> is called <i>Asirit</i>-The Tenth,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar HaKlallim Ch. 7; Shaar HaHakdamot, Sod Mitzvot Aseh 179a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2, pg. 795; Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 883.</i> because it is taken from the tenth of each of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, that is, from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of each <i>Sefirah</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>.
For example, from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> is drawn down and from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> the <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Malchut</i> is drawn down etc. And in this manner, all ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> are constructed.
Now, the explanation of the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of the nine <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> is as known; that it is the aspect of the revelation of each quality and <i>Sefirah</i> as it comes forth in an aspect of revelation as a tangible existence (<i>Yesh</i>) that is recognizable etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaZaken al Parshiot HaTorah Vol. 1, pע. 408; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, pg. 215; Kuntreisim pg. 353; Torat Chayim, Miketz 215b.</i>
An example is the quality of love when it comes forth into tangible revelation etc.
Now, this aspect of essential revelation is called the essential image (<i>Tzelem</i>-צלם) and form, like the essential image of a seal and the like, or like the form of the face itself etc.
This refers to the aspect of the organs (vessels) of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, regarding which it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Tikunei Zohar,</i> Introduction, 3b.</i> “He and His organs are one,” which is like the matter of the potential power to limit, as explained previously (in chapter twenty-nine).
However, the aspect of Likeness-<i>Demut</i>-דמות is in <i>Nukvah</i>-the female of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, which is [only] called the,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 1:28</i> “<b>likeness</b> (<i>Demut</i>-דמות) of the glory of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה,” which is <i>Zeir Anpin</i>.
This is as known regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:26; See Zohar III 35b; Maamarei Admor HaZaken al Parshiot HaTorah Vol. 1 pg. 173; 5563 Vol. 2 pg. 670; Shaarei Teshuvah 106d; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2 pg. 553</i> “Let us make man in our form (<i>Tzalmeinu</i>-<b>צלמ</b>ינו) and in our likeness (<i>Dmuteinu</i>-<b>דמות</b>ינו),” that <i>Tzelem</i>-Form refers to the male, whereas <i>Demut</i>-Likeness refers to the female (<i>Nukvah</i>) etc.
This is like the matter of letters that are engraved etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 15b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot Vol. 1, pg. 159</i> which is the aspect of a revelation of a revelation, like the letters of a seal that are imprinted into wax, and the like etc.
Similarly, the aspect of the revelation of the essential qualities of the heart, when they come forth in an aspect of revelation and tangibility in the speech of the five organs of the mouth, they become an aspect of an independent separate entity which is called <i>Yesh D'Yesh</i>-Something of something, as explained elsewhere at length.
For example, the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Chessed</i> in the heart which comes into revelation in a limited manner, is nevertheless still connected and unified with the essence of <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Chessed</i> etc.
In contrast, its revelation in speech, as in the saying,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:3</i> “Let there be light (<i>Yehiy Ohr</i>-יהי אור),” is a separate, independent thing, which is the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Malchut</i> that is drawn from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Chochmah</i> of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> in a manner of particulars.
The same is true with the construction of all of the specific ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> with their lights and vessels into an independent <i>Partzuf</i>-stature etc.
However, prior to the <i>Nesirah</i>-Separation they were two (ד”ו) statures [in one], similar to one’s back, which follows one’s front and has no independent existence of its own.
Likewise, the aspect of the revelation of <i>Malchut</i> was included in the back (<i>Achorayim</i>) of each <i>Sefirah</i> [of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>], because,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Bava Kama 74a</i> “Two hundred includes [one hundred] etc.”
(This accords with what is explained elsewhere<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">See Sefer Hamaamarim 5563 p. 223ץ</i> regarding the details of the matter of <i>Achor B’Achor</i>-Back to Back, and <i>Achor B’Panim</i>-Back to Face etc. or the opinion that,<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Brachot 61a</i> “it was a tail” etc.)
Now at first [<i>Malchut</i>] was like a point under <i>Yesod</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> etc., as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Esther 8:3; Also see Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Inyanim, p. 213</i> “And she fell before his feet.” This is as stated in Zohar<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 191a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot Vol. 2, p. 447.</i> about the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Palms 103:3</i> “That do his word” that it made itself small like a point etc., until it was a <i>Heh-</i>ה as before.
For afterwards it is built into a <i>Partzuf-</i>stature in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>, until it becomes an aspect of <i>Panim B'Panim</i>-Face to Face etc.
This can be likened to the waning and waxing of the moon.
This then, is the primary aspect of the construction of <i>Malchut</i> as it still transcends the construction of <i>Malchut</i> as a stature within <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>, wherein the entirety of its stature, which is in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>, is concealed and only the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> penetrates the screen and becomes a stature in <i>Briyah</i>, as will be explained etc. This will suffice for the understanding.
This is the true meaning of the enlarged <i>Dalet</i>-ד of “One-<i>Echad</i>-אחד,”<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 6:4</i> which is the aspect of the maturation of the stature of the female-<i>Nukvah</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, specifically in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>, with intellect and emotions, lights and vessels.
(This is as stated [about the verse,] “And <i>HaShem Elohim-</i>יהו"ה אלהי"ם built the side”; that this refers to <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> that built her etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 2:22; Zohar <i>Bereishit</i> 48b - 49a.</i> and told her,<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar <i>Balak</i> 187a</i> “Go and guard your house,” to be the head of <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i> etc.)
(This is as known regarding the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">Numbers 21:18; See Sefer HaMaamarim 5564 p. 173.</i> “The well that the princes dug etc.”)
The explanation of the matter is that the aspect of speech of thought, discussed previously, which is the enlarged <i>Dalet</i>-ד, becomes the thought of the supernal speech of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> in an aspect of ten <i>Sefirot</i> with lights and vessels, and is from the <i>Malchut</i> of the nine <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, as mentioned above.
This then, is the meaning of [<i>Echad</i>-אחד, that is] <i>E”ch</i>-א”ח <i>Dalet</i>-ד,<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">See Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar Kriyat Shma, Shaar 8, Ch. 12.</i> as explained elsewhere at length. This is as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">30</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 2:7 and Onkelos translation there.</i> “And man became a living soul - a speaking spirit” which is,<sup class="footnote-marker">31</sup><i class="footnote">Ecclesiastes 8:4</i> “the word of the King rules” with the ten utterances of,<sup class="footnote-marker">32</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1</i> “And God said-<i>Vayomer Elohi”m-ויאמר אלהי״ם</i>,” as known.
Now, the aspect of <i>Keter</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> is the aspect of the power of speech before spreading forth in actual speech with the aspects of the intellect and emotions of speech, which are the [other] nine <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i>.
This is the explanation of the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">33</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 119:89; <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Dvarim</i> Vol. 2, p. 382</i> “Forever, <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, Your word stands in the heavens,” that is, in the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>. In other words, the aspect of the power of speech is always connected to the chest of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> etc., as stated in Etz Chayim and explained elsewhere.
The spreading forth of <i>Malchut</i> garbs <i>Tiferet, Netzach, Hod</i> and <i>Yesod</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin,</i> which is the aspect of <i>Dalet</i>-ד-four, for <i>Malchut</i> is called דל-<i>Dal</i>-poor.<sup class="footnote-marker">34</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 41:2; Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar 29 Ch. 3</i>
The root of the construction of <i>Malchut</i> is from the kindnesses (<i>Chassadim</i>) of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">35</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 16:5; Torat Chayim, Vayeitze p. 176a</i> “His throne is founded on kindness” and it is written,<sup class="footnote-marker">36</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 41:2</i> “Happy is he who considers the poor (<i>Dal-</i>דל)” and the word kindness-<i>Chessed</i>-חסד is a composite of “pity-<i>Chas</i>-חס [on the] poor-<i>Dalet</i>-דלית,”<sup class="footnote-marker">37</sup><i class="footnote">Tikkunei Zohar, Tikkun 22; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot, Vol. 2, pg. 643</i> for <i>Malchut</i> has nothing of her own,<sup class="footnote-marker">38</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 6, Ch. 6; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah, Vol. 2, pg. 511</i> only what she receives from <i>Zeir Anpin</i>.
This is as previously explained regarding the matter of a revelation of a revelation etc., or like the analogy of the moon that receives from the light of the sun, and as stated in Zohar,<sup class="footnote-marker">39</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 135b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577<i>,</i> pg. 24</i> “The moon has nothing of her own etc.”
This was not the case when <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> were equal in their statures,<sup class="footnote-marker">40</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Or HaTorah, Bereishit</i> p. 80</i> as they were before the lessening of the moon, when they were called,<sup class="footnote-marker">41</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:16; <i>Sefer HaMaamarim</i> 5565, Vol. 2, p. 593</i> “The two great luminaries,” and similarly about the coming future it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">42</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 30:26; <i>Sefer HaMaamarim</i> 5565, Vol. 2, p. 593</i> “And the light of the moon [shall be as the light of the sun] etc.”
However, there are also two levels in the construction of the female (<i>Nukvah</i>). The first is in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>, which is the matter of the separation etc., and the second is that it becomes the head of <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>.
(This is in accordance with what is written elsewhere about the statement<sup class="footnote-marker">43</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chullin 60b; Biurei HaZohar, Acharei 77b; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Maamarei RaZa”L pg. 221; 5565 Vol. 2 pg. 594.</i> “Go and lessen yourself etc.,” that this refers to the aspect of <i>Malchut,</i> which becomes the,<sup class="footnote-marker">44</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar Chadash, Shir HaShirim 71a; Etz Chayim, Shaar 3, Ch. 1; Shaar 4, Ch. 6; Mamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1 p. 179.</i> “head of the foxes,” in <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>. This is as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">45</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:16</i> “the lesser luminary to rule the night.”
For in general the entire aspect of <i>Atzilut</i> is called day, whereas the quality of night refers to the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> as it becomes hidden in the head of <i>Briyah,</i> as will be explained in subsequent chapters regarding the matter of, “Blessed be the Name of His glorious Kingship forever and ever etc.,” which is after it penetrates the screen etc. This will suffice for the understanding.)

Chapter 48

Now for more detail regarding the aspect of the construction of <i>Malchut,</i> which is called “The Bride-<i>Kalah</i>-כלה,”<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Pardes Rimonim, Shaar 23, “<i>Kalah</i>-כלה.”</i> because it includes “Everything-<i>HaKol</i>-הכל” etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">See Pirush L'Maarechet Elokut, Ch. 4 (70a); Also see Torat Chayim, VaYeitze, 174b; Shaarei Teshuvah 16c.</i> this is the fact that everything becomes revealed in the aspect of speech in a tangible and separate way, like the letters of speech that reveal all.
This includes even the aspect of the essential pleasure and desire that is in the Essential Self of the light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>) literally, that is, the aspect of the <i>Heyulie</i> desire for kindness, that was previously mentioned (in chapter ten), as it chains down in its great descent, until the desire and wisdom and emotions of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> and <i>Arich Anpin</i>, until the aspect of the desire, wisdom and emotions in the external vessels of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>. All this comes into the aspect of <i>Malchut</i>, which is the aspect of the Supernal speech with a revelation of somethingness in an aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>.
Regarding this it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 44:6; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bamidbar Vol .3 p. 1,141</i> “I am first and I am last,” and it similarly states,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 32:39</i> “See that I, I am He,” that is, the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>) [vested] in <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>, which is called<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar II 56a; Zohar II 226a</i> “the end of all levels” etc.
Now, we must first understand in a detailed manner the <i>Partzuf</i>-stature of <i>Malchut</i>, from the aspect of <i>Keter</i> that is in it, until the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> that is in it, which penetrates the screen to become the <i>Keter</i> of <i>Briyah</i> etc.
For, on <i>Rosh Hashanah</i> the construction of <i>Keter</i> of <i>Nukvah</i>-the Female takes place etc., and this is why we say the ten verses of kingship etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, <i>Rosh HaShanah</i> 32a; <i>Siddur</i> of <i>Alter Rebbe, Rosh HaShanah</i>, 238b; <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Dvarim</i> Vol .4, p. 1,360; <i>Na”Ch</i> p. 502.</i>
In other words, this is in order to draw down anew the aspect of the pleasure and desire for kingship, that is, to awaken anew the aspect of the simple pleasure and desire of the Essential Self of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), that,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">See Chapter 7 &amp; 10</i> “I will rule” etc.
(This is the explanation of the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 103:20; Zohar III 191a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot, Vol. 2, p. 447.</i> “The mighty in strength that actualize His word etc.,” as mentioned in Zohar and as explained elsewhere regarding the words,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">A hymn (<i>Piyut</i>) in high holiday liturgy; See Shaarei Teshuvah 106b; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah, Vol. 2 pg. 808.</i> “And they have given You a crown of Kingship etc.”)
For as known, the aspect of the aforementioned revelation of speech is called, “The Word of The King,” and is the quality of Lordship, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 93:1</i> “<i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה reigns; He is clothed in majesty etc.,” or,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 145:13</i> “Your kingdom is a Kingship over all the worlds etc.”
This is analogous to the quality of lordship in man, which is a quality that is separate from one’s essential self, for it is specifically the quality of ruling over one’s fellow etc. This is not the case with the other qualities, which literally are part of one’s essential self.
For example, with the light of the quality of kindness, the soul itself is drawn after and becomes aroused by the kindness. For the primary essence of this quality is a drawing forth from the essential self [of the soul] and the same is true of wisdom, which is drawn from the essential self [of the soul].
However, in regard to the quality of lordship, even though the soul is aroused by it, nevertheless, it primarily comes into being by something that is separate from the self, that is, that [he rules] over his fellow, and if there were nothing aside for himself, there would be no arousal of this quality altogether.
And although the quality of kindness is also specifically in order to do kindness to his fellow, nevertheless the beginning of its arousal is within his essential self, even if there is no one to bestow his goodness to. This is not the case with [the quality] of lordship, which essentially does not come into being without someone over whom to rule.
Proof of this is from the fact that its entire construction of spreading to a length and breadth, depends solely on the submission of the people to him. When they exalt him, they arouse the ultimate depth of his dominion, but with the lessening of submission, the light of this quality likewise lessens etc.
However, with [the quality of] kindness, it will spread forth as it is in the essential self. And although there will be fluctuations of more or less [kindness] according to the manner in which the recipient arouses and requests [the kindness], with great pleading [or less pleading] etc., nevertheless, it is not primarily constructed from this etc. This will suffice for the understanding.
Now, we must understand the analogue of this as it is Above, because<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli Brachot 58a</i> “as the earthy kingdom is, so is the kingdom of Heaven,” in that,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Rabbeinu Bachaye to Genesis 38:30; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah, Vol. 2, pg. 631</i> “There is no king without a nation,” specifically.
This is because although the Lordship of the aspect of the quality of <i>Malchut</i> Above, is like the other supernal qualities, nevertheless it is not an actual drawing forth from the aspect of the Essential Self of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, the Unlimited One, blessed is He.
(However, it nonetheless is there in potential and in a state of great concealment, for even in the aspect of a human being, even a small child possesses the aspect of lordship to rule over everything, including animals, for this is his nature immediately from birth, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:28; Also see Likkutei Torah, Emor 38b; Sefer HaMaamarim 5568 Vol. 1 pg. 259, 356; Ateret Rosh 41b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Kuntreisim, pg. 314; Hanachot 5577 p. 343</i> “[And God said to them...] have dominion over [the fish of the sea and over the fowl of the air and over every living thing that creeps upon the earth] etc.”
We observe in the nature of a child, that his desire is to control and dominate over animals, beasts and birds etc., as discussed elsewhere that this is a [quality] specific to mankind. In contrast, the qualities of kindness and mercy may also be found even in the beasts, such as the eagle, which is merciful etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Yerushalmi Pe'ah 1:5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 879.</i> )
Now even though [the essential hidden quality] is called the quality of lordship, nevertheless its primary construction is specifically to have dominion over something external to himself and it is specifically then that the pleasure and great desire to rule is drawn out. According to this we must understand how this is applicable Above in <i>HaShem’s-</i>יהו"ה Godliness, for there is nothing outside of Himself upon whom to rule etc.
Therefore, it would not be possible for there to be the aspect of the construction of <i>Malchut</i> with desire and pleasure and emotions in the aspect of a complete stature in the aspect of <i>Atzilut,</i> were it not for the arousal of His desire that there should be a being separate from Himself over whom to rule, and it is specifically then, that this quality is aroused in the Emanator.
Regarding this it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 93:1</i> “<i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה reigns, He is clothed in majesty,” that is, He vests within this quality to be a King over a nation.
It is for this reason that it is specifically this quality that must be renewed from its essential source every <i>Rosh HaShanah</i>, that is, all the way to the aspect of the essential thought, “I will rule,” within the Essential Self of the light of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, the Unlimited One, blessed is He etc., which is the aspect of Lordship that arose in the aspect of His Essential Self before the <i>Tztimzum</i>-constriction.
It is for this reason that the first <i>Tzimtzum</i>-restraint, which is called the empty place<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 1, Anaf 2</i> (<i>Makom Panuy</i>), took place in order that there be something outside of His Essential Self upon which it would be applicable for the aspect of the light of Lordship of the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>) [to rule].
(This is as stated elsewhere about the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 31:12</i> “She does him good etc.,” about the root of the idolaters who He separated from His Oneness in an aspect of darkness and <i>tzimtzum</i>-restraint etc., so that there would be the quality of <i>Tiferet</i>-mercy.<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar Yitro 87a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot Vol. 2 p. 635; Torat Chayim Noach p. 75c.</i> This is because the quality of mercy likewise only applies to a person who specifically is foreign and distant etc. This will suffice for the understanding.)
In this manner we may understand the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>, the end of all levels of <i>Atzilut</i>, which is the desire and pleasure etc., of the quality of Lordship, to be the king over <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>, for which purpose it was necessary for there to be the constriction of the screen between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah,</i> for it to become the head of the foxes etc., as known.
This then, is the meaning of [“I am first, and I am last,”] that is, “I am first” in the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה Himself, blessed is He, and “I am last” in <i>Malchut</i> of Emanation-<i>Atzilut</i> for,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer Yetzirah 1:7</i> “Their beginning is bound to their end,” and this takes place each and every <i>Rosh HaShanah,</i> as known. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 49

We must now understand the specifics of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>.
That is, the aspect of the simple pleasure and desire that comes to be revealed in the light of this quality, is the aspect of the <i>Keter</i> that is within it in general, as discussed previously.
Afterwards, the light of the pleasure and desire that transcends the intellect and reasoning, becomes constricted in the aspects of the <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> for this desire. This is the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> of the quality of <i>Malchut</i>, which is called <i>Chochmah Tata'a</i>-The Lower <i>Chochmah</i> (The Wisdom of Solomon).
This is the <i>Chochmah</i> at the end, that is rooted in the <i>Chochmah</i> at the beginning,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 26b; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2 pg. 495 and on; Kuntreisim p. 212; Torat Chayim, VaYeishev 201c.</i> that is, the wisdom for this desire in the quality of <i>Malchut</i> is drawn from the aspect of <i>HaShem’s</i>-יהו"ה essential <i>Chochmah.</i>
This is the meaning of the statement that,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Rosh HaShanah 32a</i> “<i>Bereishit-</i>בראשית is also an utterance [of creation],” that is, it is the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> of the speech of the ten utterances of <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם<i>,</i> as known. This is called the aspect of the brains [or intellect] of the <i>Nukvah</i>-female of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, as known.
Afterwards, the aspect of the emotions of <i>ChaGa”T</i> and <i>NeHi”Y</i> of <i>Malchut</i> are drawn forth, like the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 29:4</i> “A King establishes [the land] with justice etc.”
(This is like what our sages stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Avoda Zara 3b; Also see Imrei Binah, Shaar HaKriyat Shma 67b.</i> “There are twelve hours in the day; three hours He sits and is occupied in the study of Torah” in the aspect of the intellect of the emotions, “three hours He sits and judges” according to the intellect, and “three hours He sits and sustains” in the aspect of <i>NeHi”Y</i> etc., as explained elsewhere at length.)
This is the meaning of the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 104:24</i> “You have actualized (<i>Asita</i>) all of them with wisdom (<i>Chochmah</i>),” for it includes all the utterances of the other specific qualities in the word of the King etc., like the <i>Yerushalmi</i> translation [on the word] <i>Bereishit-</i>בראשית meaning “With wisdom-<i>B'Chuchmeta-</i>בחכמתא,” as known.<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Targum Yerushalmi to Genesis 1:1</i>
And “He renews the act of creation every day” according to the intellect in the emotions of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> that descend into <i>Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i> each day in various novel ways as <i>Malchut</i> receives from <i>NeHi”Y</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> etc.
This is because every day new intellect is drawn forth from <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> to <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah,</i> to the point that at every hour and moment there is a renewal of the light and influence from its first source, which is the simple pleasure and desire in <i>Malchut</i> of the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, blessed is He, as it states, “Your Kingship [is the Kingship of all worlds] etc.,” as known.
Now at times, the aspect of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> are in an aspect of immaturity (<i>Katnut</i>) and at times they are in an aspect of maturity (<i>Gadlut</i>).
