This is similar to what was explained previously about the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>; that they have mature and immature intellect [depending on how they receive from] the emotions of <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> etc., even [including] the ultimate immaturity in the external vessels of <i>NeHi”Y</i> etc.
Likewise in the aspect of the revelation of <i>Malchut,</i> as it is built into an independent stature, at times there is an aspect of mature intellect in the emotions from the aspect of <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> of <i>Malchut</i>. This is like when the intellect spreads forth abundantly in the emotions that are revealed in speech.
At other times, however, it radiates in an aspect of immaturity, so much so, that sometimes the emotions of <i>Malchut</i> are in a state of complete immaturity.
(This is as stated in Zohar about the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Song of Songs 1:5; Zohar <i>Balak</i> 191a; <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shmot</i> Vol. 2, p. 447.</i> “I am black etc.” that she made herself small and became like a point etc., which refers to the point under <i>Yesod,</i> as it states, “And she fell before his feet” as discussed previously.)
(This is also like the difference between the days of the week and Shabbat, for Shabbat receives from the aspect of <i>ChaGa”T</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i>, as in,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Piyut Azamer Bishvachin</i>, Shabbat evening prayers</i> “The right, the left, and the bride in between them etc.” At times [influence] is received in an aspect of face to face (<i>Panim B'Panim</i>), such as on <i>Yom Kippur,</i> when <i>Malchut</i> ascends to the inner aspect of <i>Atik Yomin</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Dvarim</i> Vol. 3, p. 1,105</i>)
Now, the aspect of the vessels of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> is the aspect of the letters of speech of the ten utterances [of creation] and there are three levels in this, just as we described previously about thought.
That is, thought of speech is the aspect of the vessel for the <i>ChaBa”D</i> of <i>Nukvah</i>, and speech of speech is the aspect of the vessel of the breath of speech [that conveys] the emotions of speech, and action of speech is the aspect of the vessel of <i>NeHi”Y</i> of <i>Malchut,</i> until the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> that penetrates the screen etc.
The explanation of the matter is as known, that thought of speech can be compared to the thought that becomes garbed within speech, when a person speaks about something, that it is certain that in every particular word, there is vested the particular thought of that speech.
For the manner of the combinations of the letters of speech are patterned exactly according to the pattern of the combinations of thought.
(This is as discussed previously, that the heels of <i>Leah</i> enter into the head of <i>Rachel</i>; that the aspect of thought of speech is made from the aspect of speech of thought and included in this is also the thought of <i>how</i> to speak, both generally and specifically etc.)
For example, within the utterance, “Let there be light-<i>Yehiy Ohr</i>-יהי אור,” is vested the thought of this utterance.
It too is called a, “closed saying” (<i>Maamar Satoom</i>), because all that comes into [actual] revelation is only the speech of, “Let there be light-<i>Yehiy Ohr</i>-יהי אור.”
This thought is the aspect of the vessel for the <i>ChaBa”D</i> of this utterance “Let there be light-<i>Yehiy Ohr</i>-יהי אור” which is the aspect of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Malchut</i> etc., for the first thousand (of the six thousand) years<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">This will be discussed in the next chapter.</i> (as will be explained).
And the thought of the second utterance of “Let there be a firmament-<i>Yehiy Rakia</i>-יהי רקיע” is in the quality of judgment (<i>Gevurah</i>) of <i>Malchut</i>, and is the aspect of the vessel for the intellect of this quality etc.
The same applies to all the six emotive qualities of <i>Malchut</i>; that their aspect of thought is the vessel for the intellect that they contain.
And the aspect of the vessels for <i>ChaGa”T</i> and <i>NeHi”Y</i> etc. which is the aspect of speech of speech, can be compared to the letters of the kindness or judgment of the speech itself.
This is because the word and decree of the King contains these three qualities; kindness, judgment and mercy, that is, the aspect of <i>ChaGa”T</i>, and this comes into the word of the King in actual speech and letters.
Now, the wisdom and emotions that become revealed in it, are the aspect of the form (<i>Tzurah</i>) of speech, which is called the Speaking Spirit (<i>Ruach Memalela</i>) or the Speaking Soul (<i>Nefesh HaMedaberet</i>) etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">See Chapter 38</i> as known.
The aspect of action of speech, which is the vessel for <i>NeHi”Y</i> etc., is when the speech comes to give a command for actualization in actuality, such as “and God said, and it was so” in actuality.
For example, when a king commands for something to actually be done, it first begins with a decree in the words of his judgment, that are called the word and decree of the king, that include [the qualities of] <i>ChaGa”T</i>. Afterwards the final ruling comes to a command to be actualized, which is called the aspect of <i>NeHi”Y</i>, and the aspect of the vessel for this <i>NeHi”Y</i> is the letters of speech [themselves], wherein he simply commands it to be done.
(Similarly, the movement of the lips<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli 90b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, p. 910.</i> is also [considered to be] an action and is called action of speech as well, for the essence of the matter is that the mouth cuts the words of speech to come forth in actuality and completion, as there is also speech which is not yet for action etc.)
It is in this regard that it states, “And God said, ‘Let there be light’” and “[let there be] a firmament,” specifically in action.
Now the aspect of the action that resulted from this speech, is as written, “And there was light-<i>Vayehiy Ohr</i>-ויהי אור” and the like, is like when the word of the king is really actualized, and this is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>.
This only occurs when the influence and light, comes forth to be an aspect of a source for the actual creation of something from nothing etc. This is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut,</i> which penetrates the screen to become a source for <i>Briyah</i>-creation, as will be explained. This will suffice for the understanding.
(However, this too is still in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i> and is called the aspect of <i>Asiyah-</i>action of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>.
For example, this is like the power in the action that is separate from the power of the one who acts, for although the power of the one who acts is an aspect of the power of actualization, nevertheless, the power that comes out from his power into the acted upon, is the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i>, as explained elsewhere.)

Chapter 50

Now, it is known regarding the particulars of the matter of the five judgments<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 1, pg. 237</i><i>MaNTzePa”Ch</i> (מנצפ״ך) of speech in the ten utterances [of creation] that<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Introduction to Zohar 2a</i> “the mother lends [to the daughter],” that these are the five organs of [speech of] the mouth.
[The letters] <i>Aleph-</i>א<i>, Chet-</i>ח<i>, Heh-</i>ה<i>, Ayin-</i>ע are from the throat, <i>Gimel-</i>ג<i>, Yod-</i>י<i>, Chaf-</i>כ<i>, Kof-</i>ק are from the palate,<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer Yetzirah 2:1; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 2 &amp; 3 (The Letters of Creation) and Vol. 4 (The Vowels of Creation); Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee Dvarim Vol. 1, p. 105</i> and so forth, so that there are specific letters for each organ, in and of itself.
The combinations arise through their union and intermingling in various different manners.
This is in accordance with what it states in Sefer Yetzirah,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer Yetzirah 2:3; Sefer Yetzirah 4:5 and on; Sefer Yetzirah 4:12</i> “And He set them in the mouth etc., He made [the] letter [<i>Aleph-</i>א] reign etc., go out and contemplate that from five letters, one hundred and twenty combinations are made etc.”
This comes about by means of the aspect of the five judgments that divide the breath of speech.
For in speech there is substance (<i>Chomer</i>) and form (<i>Tzurah</i>). The breath of the voice of speech is the substance, which is comprised of fire, water and wind (אמ”ר),<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar II 184b; Ginat Egoz translated as HaShem Is One ibid.; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee<i>,</i> Vayikra Vol. 2, p. 651; Torat Chayim 39d.</i> and the voice is divided into various combinations. Nonetheless, a single voice unites the totality of all the combinations.
(This is as explained elsewhere about the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Song of Songs 1:10; See Maamarei Admor HaZaken 5564 pg. 9; Ketuvim Vol. 2, pg. 89; Likkutei Torah, Shir HaShirim 13a.</i> “Your neck with [a necklace of] beads” that it is like the single strand that unifies and binds the many stones of a necklace together.
It is likewise so, regarding the aspect of the letters of thought in speech, that there is a single general thought that encompasses and unifies all the particular letters of thought that [come out] in the particulars of speech.
The same is likewise so in regard to the voice of thought itself and the five judgments of <i>Imma</i> etc.)
Now, as known<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III (Raaya Mehemna) 256b, 248a; 258a; Tanya Igeret HaKodesh 5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, pg. 380, Kuntreisim pg. 547 and on.</i> “The father founded the daughter” as stated that the [power of] combination is of <i>Chochmah</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch</i> p. 120; <i>Kuntreisim</i> p. 547.</i>
This is in accordance with what was previously explained regarding thought, that is, that the combinations of speech themselves are by means of the aspect of the five judgments that restrain the manner that the intellect [is revealed] in speech, and that it is specifically according to this, that the combinations are drawn forth.
Therefore, the various different ways that the combinations [of speech] constantly change, is precisely according to the dictates of the intention of the thought that is [vested] in the speech.
The above explains the statement that it is specifically <i>Imma</i> that “lends [the clothes] etc.,” which is the aspect of <i>Binah</i> – that is, the upper <i>Imma</i> – that is drawn into the lower <i>Imma,</i> which is the aspect of <i>Binah</i> that becomes vested within the thought of speech, that is, within the specific manner of each combination of speech etc.
However, the statement that, “the [power of] combination is of <i>Chochmah,</i>” refers to the root and power to actually combine these various combinations that are in accordance to the intellect of <i>Binah</i>.
For, we observe that immediately upon the arousal of one’s desire to speak in various specific combinations, one need not delve into the intellect and comprehension of <i>Binah</i> to determine how to combine the letters, for even a small child who speaks, immediately knows to combine the letters of speech, without any preparation for it whatsoever.
This is because the root of this power to combine comes spontaneously from the radiance of the <i>Koach Ma”H</i> (כח מ״ה) of <i>Chochmah</i> (חכ<b>מה</b>) that transcends the comprehension of <i>Binah</i>. That is, it is from the aspect of the power of the intellect (<i>Koach HaMaskeel</i>) itself, which is the source of <i>Chochmah</i>.
(This is as explained elsewhere regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Gensis 2:7; See Torah Or, Miketz 42b; Derech Mitzvotecha pg. 75;</i> “And the man became a living soul [<i>Nefesh Chayah</i>],” which is the inner aspect of the beginnings of <i>Chochmah</i>, and that it is specifically then that he is able to speak and is called a “<i>Ruach Memalela</i> – a speaking spirit etc.”)
This then, [explains] the statement that, “the father founded the daughter,” as known.
(In this respect, the statement that, “<i>Bereishit</i>-בראשית is also an utterance,” refers [only] to the <i>Chochmah</i> and intellect that is within the utterances, and does not refer to the power of combination that all speakers possess, which is called the “speaking soul” etc.)
This then, is the primary aspect of a human being, who is called a “speaker” (<i>Medaber</i>), referring to the power and root of the combinations of speech, in that he is specifically called a “speaking soul” etc.
(This refers to when the aspect of the root and source of the letters of the soul themselves, come to be revealed in the aspect of the speech of the soul itself, that it is called a speaking soul (<i>Nefesh HaMedaberet</i>) or speaking spirit (<i>Ru’ach Memalela</i>) etc.)
According to this we may understand the matter of the changes in the combinations of the six days of creation of the emotive qualities of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>.
For example, the combination of the first day, “Let there be light-<i>Yehiy Ohr-</i>יהי אור,” which is the aspect of <i>Chessed</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:3; See Or HaChayim to Zohar Bereishit 46a; Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shaar HaKriyat Shma 76b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,446; Hanachot 5577 pg. 10; Torat Chayim, Bereishit 8c.</i> is the root of the first millennium of <i>Briyah, Yetzirah,</i> and <i>Asiyah,</i> as known regarding the verse, “In six days [<i>HaShem</i>] made etc.,” referring to the six upper days of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> etc., that are called,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 63:11; Deuteronomy 32:7; See Zohar III 15a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 1, pg. 225; Bamidbar Vol. 2 pg. 366.</i> “<i>Yemei Olam -</i> the days of the world” [in the masculine] and “<i>Yemot Olam</i> - the days of the world” [in the feminine].
And from the combinations of the second day,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 1:6</i> “Let there be a firmament-<i>Yehiy Rakia</i>-יהי רקיע,” come the aspect of judgment of <i>Malchut</i>, which is the source for the second millennium.
This is as known regarding the explanation of [the verse,]<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 90:4; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch pg. 398; Devarim Vol. 1, pg. 207; Vol. 3, pg. 805.</i> “For a thousand years [in Your eyes] are but a day of yesterday etc.,” referring to the<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Rosh HaShanah 31a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit p. 53.</i> “six thousand years [that] the world exists,” which are drawn from the six emotions of <i>Malchut</i> etc., that is, from the different changes in the combinations of the speaking spirit of <i>Malchut</i>, which is called the speaking soul, as in “And God said-<i>Vayomer Elohi”m</i>-ויאמר אלהי״ם etc.”
In other words, [the changing combinations] are because of the aspect of change in the drawing forth of the intellect of <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> in the emotions, whereby the manner of the combinations automatically changes from kindness to judgment, both generally and specifically.
These [combinations] are all according to the aspect of the light of the radiance of <i>Abba</i> which founded the daughter (<i>Barta</i>), for it is the root [of the power] to combine, as discussed previously, and it transcends the light of the intellect of <i>Chochmah</i> within the speech [itself] as mentioned above.
This [even] includes specific [changes] such as how Rabbi Chaninah Ben Dosa said,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Taanit 25a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot Vol. 2, pg. 332; HaNachot 5577 pg. 228.</i> “Let He who told oil to ignite [tell the vinegar to ignite] etc.” That is, let He who combined through the ten utterances of the title God-<i>Elohim-</i>אלהי״ם<i>,</i> this nature of oil to ignite; let Him say this combination and nature to vinegar, so that it should ignite.
This is as stated that,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Samuel II 23:3</i> “The righteous (<i>Tzaddik</i>) rules with his fear of God-<i>Elohi”m</i>-אלהי״ם,” that is, with the one hundred and twenty combinations of <i>HaShem’s-</i>יהו"ה title <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם,<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">See Etz Chayim, Shaar 15, Ch. 6; Shaar 44, Ch. 5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee Shemot Vol. 1, pg. 137.</i> as known.
The primary aspect of this “ruling” are the changes in the manner of the intellect of <i>Nukvah</i>, that is, the <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> that is within the ten utterances from the very root of the wisdom and the root of the desire.
This is as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 135:6</i> “Everything that <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה desired He did” with the ten utterances of the supernal speech of <i>Atzilut</i>, in the aspect of <i>Asiyah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> discussed previously.
From all of the above we may also understand the general [principle and unity of the] <i>Hitbonenut</i>-contemplation, with all its numerous details, that is, from the very root of the desire in <i>Malchut</i> of the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, blessed is He, until <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> and until the very final action, so that it literally is [understood] that “Everything that <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה desired He did” in actuality, like actually making vinegar ignite, and the like. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 51

We must now understand the matter of the screen (<i>Masach</i>) that is between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 42, Ch. 13-14; Torah Or Lech 12c;</i> and [that] <i>Malchut</i> penetrates the screen etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 42, Ch. 13; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim, Vol. 3, pg. 881;</i> as mentioned previously.
For it is known about the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 36:10; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit p. 185; Devarim Vol. 1, p. 178; Torat Chayim Vayeshev, 205a</i> “For with You is the source of life, in Your light is light seen,” that this is called an offspring light, like a light that is seen through a screen.
That is, the primary essential light remains above the screen and there is only a glimmer from the concealed essential light that is hidden within the density of the screen and penetrates and radiates [through], which is called a glimmer of a glimmer.
This is like the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar Bereishit 15b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shmot Vol. 1; pg. 159</i> “He engraved letters etc.” which is like the form of a letter that is pressed into the wax, which is only an impression of the concealed essential letter of the seal etc.
Likewise, it is only the aspect of a glimmer of a glimmer of the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> that penetrates and is seen to radiate from within the screen etc., and becomes <i>Keter</i> of <i>Briyah</i> etc., which is the [matter of], “in Your light is light seen etc.”
Regarding this it states about the creation of the world that,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Shabbat 77b</i> “At first there was darkness and then light returned etc.,” or as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 18:12; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 1,057.</i> “He made darkness His hiding place etc.”
This is also the matter of the <i>Tzimtzum</i>-restraint of <i>HaShem</i>’s-<i>יהו״ה</i> title God-<i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 84:12; Tanya, Shaar HaYichud V'HaEmunah, translated as The Gate of Unity and Faith, Ch. 4; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Dvarim Vol. 2, p. 400; Na”Ch p. 395; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 1, The Gate of Intrinsic Being (<i>Shaar HaHavayah</i>) and The Gate of His Title (<i>Shaar HaKinuy</i>).</i> “For <i>HaShem Elohi”m-</i>יהו"ה אלהי"ם is a sun and a shield,” that is, it is like a sheath for the sun etc.
(This is as known regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Exodus 20:18; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah, Vol. 1, pg. 342; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,371; Torat Chayim Bereishit 36c; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, Vol. 1, The Gate of His Title (<i>Shaar HaKinuy</i>) and The Gate of The Name (<i>Shaar HaShem</i>).</i> “And Moshe approached the thick darkness where God-<i>Elohi”m</i>-אלהי״ם was etc.” and similarly,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Palms 91:1</i> “You who dwells in the Supernal concealment, in the shadow of the Almighty (<i>Shadai-</i>שדי) etc.” that is, the One who said to his world “<i>Dai</i>-enough.” etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chagiga 12a; Likkutei Torah, Shir HaShirim 4d; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, Vol. 1, The Gate of The Name (<i>Shaar HaShem</i>)</i>)
Now the root of the matter of this screen-<i>Masach</i> is that it is made from the aspect of the garment of the <i>Chashmal,</i> from the externality of <i>Binah,</i> that encompasses until beneath the feet of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 42, Ch. 13; Torat Chayim, Noach, 58a.</i> as previously mentioned.
This is in accordance with what is stated elsewhere about the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 31:52; <i>Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Inyanim</i> p. 313; 5567 p. 250; <i>Sefer HaMaamarim</i> 5650 p. 308; <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Drushei Chatunah</i> Vol. 2, p. 505 &amp; p. 537; <i>Torat Chayim, Vayetze,</i> 178a.</i> “This heap of stones shall be witness etc.,” that it is comparable to a heap of stones that separates etc.
This is because the essence of the matter of this screen and curtain is that it is made from the combinations of letters that are called “stones” in Sefer Yetzirah,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Sefer Yetzirah</i> 4:12; <i>Torat Chayim, Bereishit</i> 21d.</i> in which the letters are not properly ordered, are like a heap of stones, one upon the other, and are like the aspect of a screen that is woven of many threads and causes a break and separation.
This is comparable to what we observe with the letters of speech, that when they are properly ordered according to intellect, the light of the intellect clearly radiates within them, so that the recipient is able to understand [the matter] exactly as the influencer [intends].
In contrast, when they are not properly ordered, the recipient will not grasp them at all.
(This is also similar to the light of the intellect and wisdom that is concealed and hidden in an analogy or a riddle about a completely foreign matter. Nonetheless, through it, he is able to come to that intellectual light.
This too is called a penetration of the screen, similar to the light of the sun as it is seen when its rays break through the thickness of the morning mist, as explained elsewhere.)
Since there is no comparison between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i>, therefore there needed to be this aspect of the <i>Tzimtzum</i> of the screen-<i>Masach</i>.
(This is similar to how there needed to be the aspect of the first <i>Tzimtzum,</i> which is called the empty place and vacant space between the Essential Self of the light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), to be the source for the drawing down of the <i>Kav</i>-line etc., as previously explained.
Only that there, [in <i>HaShem’s</i>-יהו"ה Essential Self], it was an aspect of concealment and inclusion of the light within His Essential Self, and is called the Empty place (<i>Makom Panuy</i>), rather than an actual screen.
This was compared to the concealment of one's own expansive knowledge, at a time when he reviews it in summary etc., as discussed previously. This is because all this is still within the aspect of His Essential Self.
This is not the case from <i>Atzilut</i> to <i>Briyah,</i> because from an aspect of limitlessness to become the source of actual limitation, it is necessary for there to be a screen, in a way of complete separation.
Nevertheless, there is a great benefit in the fact that the screen itself is made by He who made the <i>Tzimtzum-</i>restraint Himself, like a person who [himself] makes the analogy for the analogue, or like one who [intentionally] mixes the order of the letters and the like, because of which, this separation of the screen is not a true break or separation for himself, but only in relation to the recipients.
This is analogous to a snail whose garment is of himself and part of himself etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">See Bereishit Rabba 21:5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2, pg. 721.</i> as explained in Tanya.<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Tanya, Ch. 21</i>)
(This is the meaning of<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 44:6</i> “[I am first, and I am last].” That is, “I am first” with the first <i>Tzimtzum</i> of the empty place, and “I am last” is the final <i>Tzimtzum</i> between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i> etc., because this end action of <i>Atzilut,</i> arose first in the thought and desire of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>) etc. This will suffice for the understanding.)
Now, as known, this is the root of the matter of, “Blessed be the Name of His glorious Kingship forever and ever etc.,” which is the aspect of the “Lower Unity” (<i>Yichuda Tata'a</i>) of <i>Malchut</i>.<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Pesachim 56a; Zohar I 18b.</i>
That is, it is the radiance of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> within <i>Briyah,</i> in the aforementioned aspect of a “glimmer of a glimmer,” as it states, “In your light is light seen etc.”
Regarding this it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 4:35, 4:39</i> “<i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, He is <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי"ם etc.,” and as known regarding the statement,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar <i>Terumah</i> 135a</i> “Just as they are unified above” referring to the union of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> in the aspect of <i>Atzilut</i>, “so likewise is she unified below” referring to <i>Malchut</i> in “the Throne” (which is called) <i>Briyah</i> etc.
This then, is what the tribes, who are rooted in the six directions of <i>Briyah,</i> said to Yaakov, who is the master of the world of <i>Atzilut</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Pesachim 56a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 1,063; Shaarei Teshuvah p. 60d.</i> “Just as in your heart there is only One-<i>Echad</i>-אחד” – in the aspect of the upper unity of <i>Atzilut,</i> wherein He and His life force and His organs are one – “So likewise in our hearts there is only One-<i>Echad</i>-אחד,” in the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut,</i> as it is in <i>Briyah</i> in the lower unity.
This is the meaning of<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Zachariah 14:9; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit pg. 537.</i> “<i>HaShem-</i>יהו״ה is One and His Name is One,” as known.
In general, this is called<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar III 129a; Zohar III 11a &amp; 11b; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah Vol. 2, pg. 524; Torat Chayim, Noach 64c.</i><i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה and <i>Adon”ai-</i>אדנ"י or <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה and <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי"ם,<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">See Zohar III 129a; Zohar I 22a; Zohar III 65a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee Vayikra Vol. 1, pg. 307.</i> referring to [how <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה] encompasses [and transcends] all worlds (<i>Sovev Kol Almin</i>), and how He permeates all worlds (<i>Memaleh Kol Almin</i>).<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">See at great length in Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 1, The Gate of Intrinsic Being (<i>Shaar HaHavayah</i>), The Gate of His Title (<i>Shaar HaKinuy</i>), and The Gate of His Sanctuary (<i>Shaar HaHeichal</i>).</i>
These [aspects] are also called by the names <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה (יו״ד ה״א וא״ו ה״א) and <i>Ba”N-</i>ב״ן (יו״ד ה״ה ו״ו ה״ה). The name of <i>Ma”H-</i>מ״ה refers to<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 17, Ch. 4</i> <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and the name <i>Ba”N-</i>ב״ן is in <i>Malchut</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 18, Ch. 3; Shaar 29, Ch. 2; Shaar 34, Ch. 2 Klal 13; Shaar 39, Drush 7.</i> as they come forth in a way of expansion (<i>Miluy</i>) and expansion of expansion (<i>Miluy D'Miluy</i>) etc.
(The matter of expansions (<i>Miluy</i>) is known by way of example from the letter <i>Yod</i>-י. When it is pronounced (as a word) it has an expansion of <i>Vav</i> and <i>Dalet</i> (<i>Yod</i>-יו"ד), which is the explanation and expansion of the point of the written letter <i>Yod</i>-י.
And when one needs to explain the expansion of the <i>Vav</i>-ו and <i>Dalet</i>-ד, they too expand into additional letters of <i>Vav-</i>וא”ו and <i>Dalet</i>-דלי”ת. And so on with the expansions of the <i>Vav</i>-וא”ו and <i>Dalet</i>-דלי”ת until there are multiple expansions upon expansions (<i>Miluy D'Miluy</i>) etc.
All this is merely the flow and chaining down of the ray of light and influence as it comes in a manner of the specifics of the specifics, from concealment into revelation, and revelation upon revelation, until the final most specific detail.
This is similar to what is explained elsewhere regarding the matter of, “He spoke three thousand analogies” which are like the multitude of combinations that come in a way of chaining down, one after the other, each one internal to the next, like an analogy to an analogue, that descends and chains down. For, [even] the analogy for this analogue, itself requires an analogy, as stated in the Zohar.<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar II 145a; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah, Vol. 1, pg. 350; Torat Chayim Lech Lecha 81d; Also see Sefer HaMashalim of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as The Book of Allegories.</i>
This is likewise the matter of the expansions (<i>Miluy</i>)<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">See Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shacharit 51a; Biurei HaZohar, Tisa 53a and on.</i> that come into revelation from concealment, like a specific detail that comes forth from a general principle etc.
There is also the aspect of expansion in the opposite sense, in which there is concealment upon concealment, as explained elsewhere that this is the matter of the garment of the screen-<i>Masach</i> etc. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 52

Now, in regard to the aspect of the specifics of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> as they are in <i>Briyah</i> after penetrating the screen (<i>Masach</i>), it is known that the aspect of <i>Keter Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> which is called <i>Atik</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> is what is drawn forth from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> etc., and is the aspect of the desire and pleasure for the aspect of the source of actual creation (<i>Briyah</i>) of something from nothing.
This is like the statement,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar I 86b</i> “When it arose in His will to create the world,” for just as it arose in His will to emanate (<i>Atzilut</i>) etc., so likewise His will descended to create something from nothing etc., and this is what is called <i>Keter Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah</i>.
(This is as explained elsewhere regarding the matter of,<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Brachot 7a; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, EtHalech Liozhna pg. 70; Inyanim pg. 382; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit pg. 25; Na”Ch p. 599; Drushei Chatunah Vol. 1, pg. 261.</i> “Yishmael my son, bless Me; and he answered Him, “May it be desirable before You etc.” That is, Rabbi Yishmael, the High Priest, was in the Holy of Holies of <i>Briyah</i>-Creation, wherein there descends the light of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut,</i> to become the Crown (<i>Keter</i>) of <i>Briyah</i>-Creation. He therefore said to him, “My son, bless Me (<i>Barcheini</i>-ברכני)”<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">The term “<i>Brachah</i>-ברכה” also means “to draw down” (see Mishnah Kilayim 7:1).</i> to which he responded, “may it be desirable before You etc.”)
From this pleasure and desire to bring about the creation (<i>Briyah</i>) etc., it was drawn down [further] into <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> of this desire and pleasure, which are called <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> of <i>Briyah</i>.
From <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma,</i> which are the aspects of <i>Chochmah</i> and <i>Binah</i> of this desire and pleasure, the emotions, which are called <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> were drawn down.
From <i>Zeir Anpin</i> [it was drawn down] to <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> which is the source that brings the world of <i>Briyah,</i> with its souls and angels, into being from nothing into actual something etc.
Similarly, in the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Briyah</i> there also is the aspect of lights (<i>Orot</i>) and vessels (<i>Kelim</i>), garments (<i>Levushim</i>) and chambers (<i>Heichalot</i>).
This is as known regarding the seven chambers<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 40, Drush 13</i> (<i>Heichalot</i>) of <i>Briyah</i>-Creation;<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">See Sefer HaMaamarim 5565, pg. 805; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, BaMidbar Vol. 3, pg. 995 and on.</i> that the union of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> occurs in the chamber of the Holy of Holies, which is the seventh chamber<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar II (<i>Heichalot</i>) 258b; Etz Chayim, Shaar 46, Ch. 1 &amp; 5</i> etc.
Now, from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> the aspect of <i>Keter</i> and <i>Atik Yomin</i> of the world of <i>Yetzirah</i><sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 46, Ch. 2, 5, and 6.</i> made, and this too is through the penetration of a screen (<i>Masach</i>) between <i>Briyah</i> and <i>Yetzirah</i>, similar to what was previously discussed regarding the screen between <i>Atzilut</i> and <i>Briyah</i>.
For, just as it arose in His desire to create, so likewise did it arise in his desire to form (<i>Yetzirah</i>) and to actualize (<i>Asiyah</i>), only that it is necessary for there to be a break and a screen between the end action of the desire for <i>Briyah</i>-Creation and the beginning of the desire for <i>Yetzirah</i>-Formation.
This is as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 43:7</i> “For My glory I have created it (<i>Barativ</i>), I have formed it (<i>Yatzartiv</i>), I even have actualized it (<i>Af Asitiv</i>).”
Now, as known, the [worlds of] Creation-<i>Briyah</i>, Formation-<i>Yetzirah</i>, and Action-<i>Asiyah</i> are called the three separate worlds [that] actually [come into being in a manner of] something from nothing.
This is similar to the coming into being of the letters of thought, speech and action, which truly come forth in a way of tangible somethingness (<i>Yesh</i>), separate from oneself.<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577 pg. 202</i>
Likewise, from the aspect of the letters of thought of the Godly emotions of <i>Briyah,</i> which is called <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> as mentioned above, there was created the aspect of the “hidden worlds that are not revealed,” which are the souls and angels of the world of <i>Briyah,</i> [that are] actually [brought into being in a manner of] something from nothing.
For example, the soul of,<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 51:8</i> “Avraham who loves Me,” is from the aspect of the inner vessels of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of [the world of] <i>Briyah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Tanya, Igeret HaKodesh<i>,</i> Epistle 15; Sefer HaMaamarim 5565 Vol. 2, pg. 276.</i> and [the angel] <i>Michael</i> of the world of <i>Briyah</i> is from the aspect of the externality of the vessels and letters of <i>Chessed</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Briyah</i> etc.
Similarly, the upper garden of Eden (<i>Gan Eden HaElyon</i>) of [the world of] <i>Briyah,</i> is from the aspect of the light of <i>Keter</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> which is the Supernal pleasure that is called <i>Atik</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> as it constricts within <i>Binah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah</i>, wherein the souls in <i>Briyah</i> derive pleasure from the ray etc.
(As known,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Tikkunei Zohar, Tikkun 6, 23a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, pg. 262; Kuntreisim pg. 423.</i> “The supernal mother (<i>Imma</i>) settles in the throne,” which refers to the [descent of the] light of <i>Binah</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> through multitudes of chainings-down until <i>Binah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> [settles] within <i>Binah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah</i> etc. In this same manner <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> settles in [the world of] <i>Yetzirah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Tikkunei Zohar, Tikkun 6, 23a; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, HaKtzarim pg. 552; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch, pg. 14.</i> and <i>Malchut</i> settles in [the world of] <i>Asiyah</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Tikkunei Zohar, Tikkun 6, 23a</i>)
This is likewise the case in regard to the matter of the <i>Serafim</i> [angels] that are in the world of <i>Briyah</i> etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 40, Drush 13</i> They are the,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Or HaTorah, Acharei Vol. 2, pg. 540</i> “Sons of <i>Elohim</i> who stand before <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה,” which is the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of [the world of] <i>Briyah</i>.
The aspect of the vessels of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Briyah</i> is the aspect of <i>Metat”ron-</i>מטטרו״ן,<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Yevamot 16b in Tosefot; Shaarei Teshuvah 29b.</i> the minister of the world of <i>Briyah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 217a-b, and commentary of Rabbi Chayim Vital there; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch p. 334</i> about whom it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Exodus 23:21; Talmud Bavli, Sanhedrin 38b</i> “For My Name is within him” which is the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of [the world of] <i>Atzilut</i> etc.
(He is called a lad<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">See Tosefot to Yevamot 16b referenced above.</i> (<i>Na'ar</i>-נער) or the “small face [or stature]” relative to the “large face [or stature]” of the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chagiga 13b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaeee, Dvarim Vol. 3, pg. 901; Kuntreisim pg. 343.</i> as known.)
In general, the world of <i>Briyah</i> is called the “World of Thought,” which is the aspect of the concealed worlds etc.
(This is similar to [the statement that,<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Menachot 29b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bamidbar Vol. 3, p. 1,255.</i>] “The coming world was created with a <i>Yod</i>-י” which refers to the <i>Yod</i> of the thought of <i>Binah</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Briyah</i> etc., “and with a <i>Heh</i>-ה this world was created” [which refers to] the aspects of <i>Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>.)
The world of <i>Yetzirah</i>, however, is the “World of Speech,” that is, the revealed worlds etc.
(This is like the [difference between] the prophecies of Isaiah regarding the <i>Serafim</i> [angels] of <i>Briyah,</i> who say,<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 6:3</i> “Holy, [Holy, Holy etc,]” and the [prophecies] of Ezekiel regarding the <i>Chayot</i> [angels] and <i>Ophanim</i> [angels] who say, “Blessed [be the Glory of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה from His place] etc.”<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 3:12; Talmud Bavli, Chulin 92a and Tosefot there; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577 pg. 22.</i>)
Now, just as it was explained above regarding the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Briyah</i>, it is the same way with the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Yetzirah</i> and the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Asiyah</i> to the finest particulars, with lights and vessels, garments and chambers etc. and the coming into being of angels and souls in <i>Yetzirah</i>; for example [the angel] <i>Sandal”fon-</i>סנדלפו״ן etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 47, Ch. 6; Torat Chayim, Vayera 99c.</i>
For, all the prophecies of the prophets were from the aspects of <i>Netzach</i> and <i>Hod</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Yetzirah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch pg. 192.</i> as known.
And in the same manner there is a screen that separates between <i>Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 42 referenced above.</i> and the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Yetzirah</i> becomes <i>Keter</i> and <i>Atik Yomin</i> for <i>Asiyah</i>, regarding which it states, “Everything that <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה desired He did (<i>Asah</i>).”
This refers to the souls and angels of [the world of] <i>Asiyah</i>, including the aspect of the lower garden of Eden (<i>Gan Eden HaTachton</i>), until the <i>Ophanim-</i>אופנים angels who receive from the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Asiyah,</i> as known.
And it is from the aspect of the excretions of the <i>Ophanim</i> angels<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, pg. 484, Torat Chayim, Noach 59d.</i> that influence is drawn down to influence the cycles of the constellations (<i>Mazalot-</i>מזלות), which are the root of all inanimate, plant life, animals and humans, in all climates,<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">See note of the Rebbe to Sefer HaMaamarim 5708, p. 204 and Igrot Kodesh Vol. 19, p. 239; Also see Ginat Egoz of Rabbi Yosef Gikatilla, translated as HaShem Is One, Vol. 2 &amp; 3 (The Letters of Creation).</i> as well as the root for the composition of the foundational elements of fire, air, water and earth from spirituality to physicality etc.
This is similar to the statement,<sup class="footnote-marker">30</sup><i class="footnote">See Shaar HaEmunah 61a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2, p. 634; Shaarei Teshuva 20a.</i> “A land that cultivates wise [people] etc.,” because [it receives from] the <i>Mazal</i> of <i>Machkim</i> [<i>Chochmah</i>-Wisdom] etc.,<sup class="footnote-marker">31</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Shabbat 156a</i> or [the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">32</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 33:14</i>] “The choice fruits of the sun etc.,” to the point that there is even a <i>Mazal</i> for inanimate objects, as in [the statement],<sup class="footnote-marker">33</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chulin 40a</i> “the luck of the mountain,” until there is even a <i>Mazal</i> for the inanimate of the inanimate, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">34</sup><i class="footnote">Bereishit Rabba 10:6; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 848 &amp; 876 and on.</i> “There is not a blade of grass that does not have its <i>Mazal.</i>”
The constellations (<i>Mazalot</i>) are ruled by the aspect of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>, as known regarding the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">35</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 103:19</i> “His Kingdom rules over all etc.,” and as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">36</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 145:13; Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shacharit p. 53d.</i> “[Your Kingdom is the Kingdom of all worlds” and “Your dominion [is throughout all ages”] etc., as will be explained with the help of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה.

Chapter 53

Now after all the above, a person who contemplates it, will understand the general point of the entire <i>Hitbonenut</i> – contemplation, from the simple essential desire [that arose] in the actual Essence of the Light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One, because of the aspect of the essential desire for kindness that arose in His simple will (as discussed in chapter ten) etc., all the way to the aspect of the most final desire, which is the aspect of the desire to bring the world of <i>Asiyah-</i>Actuality into being, both generally and specifically, and is called <i>Keter</i> and <i>Atik Yomin</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>, regarding which it states, “Everything that <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה desired, He did (<i>Asah</i>).”
For certainly, just as it arose in His desire to have a desire and will to emanate [<i>Atzilut</i>], so likewise the desire and will to create [<i>Briyah</i>] and the desire and will to form [<i>Yetzirah</i>] and the desire and will to do [<i>Asiyah</i>], were all included in the Essence of His simple will in His Essential Self.
For example, this is just as when it arises in a person’s essential desire to have a desire for some specific matter; although this desire immediately divides into multiple desires from level to level, until the most final desire, which is the desire for the actual final action, nonetheless, it all arose instantaneously within his essential will etc., without divisions of levels whatsoever.
(This was explained in chapter seven, that there is no division of levels in the aspect of the <i>Keter</i> of the worlds of <i>Atzilut</i>, <i>Briyah</i>, <i>Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>, even though in the chaining down, the aspect of the <i>Malchut</i> of the upper level becomes the <i>Keter</i> of the lower level etc.)
Likewise, relative to the essence of His simple will in the aspect of the Essence of the light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), blessed is He, there is no differentiation of levels between the desire and will to emanate (<i>Atzilut</i>) and the desire and will to do (<i>Asiyah</i>) etc.
This is the meaning of,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 44:6</i> “I am first,” in the desire of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), blessed is He, which is the source for the desire to emanate (<i>Atzilut</i>), and “I am last,” in the most final desire of <i>Malchut</i> of the world of Action (<i>Asiyah</i>)<i>,</i> to bring into being the most lowly and final world, which are the <i>Ophanim</i> [angels] and the <i>Mazalot,</i> that are the root for the existence of the spirituality of the four elements of fire, air, water and earth, and the spirituality of the physical levels of inanimate, plant life and animals.
(This is as stated at the end of <i>Etz Chayim</i>), that everything is included in the verse, “Everything that <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה desired” – in His Essential Self – “He did,” which includes the entire chaining down of the <i>Kav</i>-line until the end of the world of <i>Asiyah</i>; that is, He includes them all.
[Relative to Him] it all is considered to be an action (<i>Asiyah</i>), because relative to His Essential Self the root of <i>Atzilut</i> and the root of <i>Asiyah</i> are literally equal, etc.
This then, is the meaning [of the continuation of the verse, “Everything that <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה desired He did] in the Heavens,” referring to the general encompassing light (<i>Sovev</i>) of the upper purity (<i>Tihiru Ila'ah</i>), “and in the earth,” referring to the aspect of how He fills all worlds (<i>Memaleh Kol Almin</i>) in the lower purity (<i>Tihiru Ta'taa</i>) etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">See Likkutei Torah, Naso 21c; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577 pg. 329; Kuntreisim pg. 593; Torat Chayim Vayigash 230d; Shaar HaEmunah 58a.</i> It all is equally one [before Him].
(This is as known that the heel of <i>Adam Kadmon</i> concludes at the end of <i>Asiyah</i><sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">See Tanya, <i>Igeret HaKodesh,</i> Epistle 20; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 1 pg. 15.</i> and his head is in the general thought at the beginning of the <i>Kav</i> (As it says about <i>Adam HaRishon-</i>The first man, that prior to the sin his feet were in <i>Asiyah</i> and his head was in <i>Briyah</i>),<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer HaGilgulim, Ch. 18; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Bereishit pg. 72; Vayikra Vol. 1 pg. 15, Bamidbar Vol. 4 pg. 1,456; Torat Chayim Bereishit 30a.</i> but <i>Adam Kadmon</i> [is nevertheless] called <i>Adam</i> of <i>Briyah</i>,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaZaken, beginning of Inyanim</i> that is, [created] something from nothing etc.)
(This is [also] the meaning of,<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Shacharit prayer of Shabbat and Yom Tov; Torat Chayim Bereishit 30a.</i> “Every stature shall bow before You etc.,” as discussed elsewhere.)
This then, is the primary intention of the entire contemplation of every detail within the chaining down of the <i>Kav</i>-line, from before the first <i>Tzimtzum</i>-restraint until the end of the world of <i>Asiyah</i>. That is, [the intention] is to unite everything in the simple unity, which is in the aspect of the Essence of the light of the Singular Preexistent Intrinsic Being, <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה, the Unlimited One, blessed is He, until the order of <i>HaShem’s</i>-יהו"ה Godly supervision of every detail, is engrained in one’s soul, even to the very last detail.
That is, even in the world of the planetary cycles and constellations (<i>Mazalot),</i> that only come from the nine external vessels of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Malchut</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>, [one must recognize] that it literally is only according to His simple will within the Essential Self of the light of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה, the Unlimited One (<i>Ein Sof</i>), blessed is He.
This is as we say [in our prayers],<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">Aravit prayer; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee Hanachot 5577 pg. 53, 67, 90, 163, 330.</i> “He – specifically – orders the stars in their watches within the firmament according to His will,” that is, literally according to His simple will in His Essential Self, for the aforementioned reason.
The explanation of, “in their watches,” refers<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Shaarei Teshuva</i> 20a</i> even to the aspect of the chambers of the husks of <i>Kelipat Nogah</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>; because the constellations (<i>Mazalot</i>) that are fixed in the heavens, are in the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>.
This is because the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Asiyah</i> in its aspect of lights, vessels and chambers etc., are all in an aspect of total nullification of the something (<i>Bitul HaYesh</i>) to the nothing (<i>Ein</i>) [from which they are brought into being], as known regarding the chamber of the Holy of Holies in <i>Asiyah,</i> where there is the union of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> and <i>Nukvah</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>, such as in the Holy Temple below etc.
Even the souls and angels of <i>Asiyah</i> are in a state of total nullification, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Nechemiah 9:6</i> “The hosts of the heavens bow to You,” referring to the <i>Ophanim</i> and <i>Chayot</i> [angels] of <i>Asiyah</i>.
Even the substance and vessels of the <i>Ophanim</i> are in an aspect of absolute nullification, as understood from the chariot [prophecy] of Ezekiel regarding the <i>Chayot</i> and <i>Ophanim</i> [angels] of <i>Yetzirah</i>.<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel Ch. 1</i>
Similarly, this is the case regarding the chariot of black and red horses of Zachariah's<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Zachariah 6:2</i> [prophecy, which refers to] times of exile, in which <i>Malchut</i> is vested within the seventy ministering angels<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar Bereishit 46b; Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shaar HaMilah 145c; Shaarei Teshuvah 74a.</i> of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Asiyah</i>. They too are in a state of total nullification, like a horse to its rider.
This is as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 19:1</i> “Behold <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה rides upon a swift cloud-עב קל etc.,” and as explained in the Zohar,<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar II 43a</i> that they are, “like a cloud upon which He rides etc.” This is similar to the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 10:15</i> “Can an axe glory over the One who chops with it etc.”
Even though there are many different levels in them, with numerous chainings-down, even those who receive through a multitude of screens, in an aspect of the back of the back of <i>Elohi״m-</i>אלהי״ם, from the forty-eight (מ”ח) last combinations [of <i>Elohi”m-</i>אלהי״ם] which is called,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Blessing of “<i>Emet V'Emunah</i>”; Pri Etz Chayim, Shaar Chag HaMatzot, Shaar 21, Ch. 5; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 1, pg. 327; Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 1,061; Shaar HaEmunah 30a &amp; 49a.</i> “the land of the children of Cham (ח”ם-48),” in a way of ultimate concealment and <i>Tzimtzum</i>-restraint with various different types of screens and separations, so much so, that it is called a garment of sackcloth and skin, as in the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 50:3; Also see <i>Siddur</i> Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Milah 45c; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2 pg. 896.</i> “I will enclothe the heavens with darkness and I will put sackcloth as their covering etc.,” as known, and as stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Havdalah</i> prayer; Shaarei Teshuva 113c</i> “He who separates etc.” Nonetheless it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 47:9</i> “God reigns over the nations etc.,” and,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Jeremiah 10:7</i> “Who will not fear You, O King of the nations etc.,” for,<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 103:19</i> “His kingdom rules over all.”
Proof of this is from Bilaam, who was the, “evil aspect of <i>Nogah”</i> (<i>Ra D’Nogah</i>), the aspect of <i>Da'at</i> of the external husks<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 194a; Etz Chayim, Shaar 32, Ch. 2; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, p. 643.</i> (<i>Kelipah</i>), as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">Numbers 24:16</i> “he who knows the knowledge of the Most High (<i>Yodeah Da'at Elyon</i>) etc.” Nevertheless, even he said,<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Numbers 24:13</i> “I cannot transgress the word of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה to do even the smallest thing etc.”
(Even his donkey, which was the aspect of <i>Nukvah</i> of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of the <i>Kelipah –</i> the female of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of the external husks,<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 107a; MeOrei Or, <i>Erech Aton</i> num. 138.</i> which is even more severe (for as will be explained about the opposite of holiness (<i>Sitra Achera</i>),<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Ecclesiastes 7:14; Biurei HaZohar, Pekudei 59b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Shemot Vol. 2, pg. 495; Shaarei Teshuvah 69a.</i> the aspect of the female-<i>Nukvah</i> is the most severe of them all<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 231b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch pg. 33.</i> etc.), [However even about his donkey] it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">Numbers 22:23</i> “and his donkey turned away [from the angel of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה] etc.,” and even Bilaam said,<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">Numbers 22:34</i> “If it displeases You, I shall return etc.”)
Now, although there are those [<i>Kelipot</i>-husks] that are in an aspect of total somethingness and separation, so much so, that they say,<sup class="footnote-marker">30</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 8:17</i> “My power and the strength of my hand [brought me all this affluence] etc., such as the ministering angel of Egypt who said,<sup class="footnote-marker">31</sup><i class="footnote">Ezekiel 29:3; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577, pg. 275; Bamidbar Vol. 2, pg. 814.</i> “My river is mine and I made myself etc.” and as the sages, of blessed memory, have stated,<sup class="footnote-marker">32</sup><i class="footnote">Torat Kohanim to Leviticus 26:14; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereishit pg. 98</i> “They know their master and intentionally rebel against Him.” These are from the aspect of the three totally impure husks (<i>Kelipot</i>), and they too submit at times, when <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה visits punishment upon them.
This is as explained about the various prophecies of the prophets regarding some of the ministering angels of the idolatrous nations of the world etc.
However, in the aspect of <i>Nogah</i>, even the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Asiyah,</i> which is mostly evil with a minority of good,<sup class="footnote-marker">33</sup><i class="footnote"><i>Etz Chayim, Shaar</i> 43, introduction; <i>Shaar</i> 47, Ch. 4; <i>Shaar</i> 49, Ch. 6.</i> they are in a state of constant submission, such as the planets and constellations, that are [influenced by] the seventy ministering angels about whom it also states, “The hosts of the heavens bow down to You,” and “They sing His praise every day” etc.<sup class="footnote-marker">34</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Torat Chayim, Bereishit</i> 1c.</i>
As known, this is in accordance with the reason for the constant orbit of the physical planets [and constellations] that this is due only to their forms and souls being in a constant state of praising and spiritual bowing to <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה etc., as explained elsewhere. This will suffice for the understanding.

Chapter 54

Now, in order to understand the chaining down of the “opposite side” in a detailed manner etc., in regard to the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of the husks of <i>Kelipah</i> of <i>Atzilut, Briyah, Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i> etc., we must first preface with the root of the aspect of the <i>Kelipah-</i>husks and understand what it is.
Now, it is known that the reason it is called by the name <i>Kelipah</i>-husks, is because it is likened to the husk of a fruit, which is the dross of each thing that comes about because of the admixture of good and bad etc. due to the shattering of the vessels etc. of the seven kings [of <i>Tohu</i>] who died and fell below etc.
The husk precedes the fruit,<sup class="footnote-marker">1</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar II 108b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 1, p. 209.</i> just as in the growth of any fruit, the peel always grows first. This is like the relationship of the placenta to the fetus, which comes about from the dross of the seminal drop etc.
Now, the root of these matters is known; that even within the aspect of pleasure, there is the aspect of its opposite. This is pain which is the opposite of pleasure, just as the letters <i>Nega</i>-plague-נגע are the opposite of the letters <i>Oneg</i>-pleasure-ענג.<sup class="footnote-marker">2</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer Yetzirah 2:4 and the commentaries there; Also see Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Kuntreisim p. 210; Shaar HaTeshuvah 53d.</i>
(Similarly, <i>Pesha</i>-transgression-פשע is the opposite letters of <i>Shefa</i>-abundance-שפע.<sup class="footnote-marker">3</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III (<i>Idra Rabba</i>) 133a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol.1, p. 307; Torat Chayim Bereishit 28b.</i>)
This is because certainly, everything that comes into an aspect of spreading forth from the essence, has its opposing power, which also comes from the essence.
Therefore, even the aspect of the spreading forth of the light of pleasure and desire has an opposing power that opposes it. For example, this is when one is prevented from delighting in that pleasure. Likewise, if there is something in opposition, which is the opposite of that pleasure, it is called pain and suffering etc.
Likewise, within the wisdom and reason for the pleasure and desire there automatically is an opposing reason that opposes the desire. This is likewise so of emotions and thought, speech and action etc.
This is like a servant who transgresses and opposes the will of his master. In doing so, he opposes all the particulars included in the will [of his master] etc.
Similarly, [it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">4</sup><i class="footnote">Ecclesiastes 7:14</i>] “God made one thing opposite the other etc.,” so that there should be an aspect of opposition. This is called the dross (<i>Pesolet</i>), the husk (<i>Kelipah</i>) and the concealment that preceded at first etc.
This comes about by means of the aspect of the <i>Tzimtzum</i> and concealment that precedes all light and influence of desire, pleasure and wisdom etc.
This is like [the verse,<sup class="footnote-marker">5</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 7:11</i>] “Who knows the strength of Your anger and Your wrath is like the fear due You etc.” This is the aspect of the opposition to the desire. It is there that anger and wrath are applicable to those who oppose and transgress the will etc., until,<sup class="footnote-marker">6</sup><i class="footnote">Jeremiah 23:19 &amp; 30:23</i> “The wrath of <i>HaShem-</i>יהו"ה shall rest upon the heads of the wicked etc.”
(This is as explained elsewhere about the matter of, “At first there was darkness [and then the light returned],” therefore,<sup class="footnote-marker">7</sup><i class="footnote">See <i>Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereshit</i> p. 179; <i>Torat Chayim, Vayishlach</i> 185a.</i> “The insolent amongst the nations of the world are powerful at first etc.”)
Now, it is known that the principal shattering [which brought about] an admixture of actual good and evil, was in the aspect of <i>Sa”G-</i>ס״ג (יו״ד ה״י וא״ו ה״י), which is the aspect of the seven lower <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Binah</i>.
These are the aspect of the emotions of the intellect that give rise to the emotions of the heart, including bad emotions, such as anger, murderousness, evil lusts, evil love and fear, conquest and boastfulness for [the sake of] evil etc.
However, in <i>Chochmah</i> there was no shattering.<sup class="footnote-marker">8</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 8, Ch. 2, Ch. 3, Ch. 6</i> Rather, only the externality of <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> fell,<sup class="footnote-marker">9</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 8, Ch. 2, Ch. 3, Ch. 6; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 3, pg. 1,116.</i> this being the root of external wisdoms [and sciences].<sup class="footnote-marker">10</sup><i class="footnote">See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 1, pg. 9; Vol. 4, pg. 1,225; Na”Ch pg. 365; Sefer HaMaamarim 5649, pg. 267.</i>
Now, [in <i>Chochmah</i>] too there is the matter of [the verses],<sup class="footnote-marker">11</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 8:12; See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 2, pg. 532; Torat Chayim, Noach pg. 79a</i> “I am wisdom, I dwell with craftiness,” or,<sup class="footnote-marker">12</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 8:12; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Devarim Vol. 4, pg. 1,496.</i> “My father was [nearly] destroyed by the Aramite,” which refers to <i>Chochmah</i> of the <i>Kelipah</i>-husks, that is only for the sake of wickedness, as in,<sup class="footnote-marker">13</sup><i class="footnote">Jeremiah 4:22</i> “They are wise to do evil,” but not to do good whatsoever. This is not true <i>Chochmah</i>-wisdom, but rather only craftiness and falsehood, as known.
Even from the aspect of the “Supernal Pleasure,” the aspect of its externality was lowered.<sup class="footnote-marker">14</sup><i class="footnote">Etz Chayim, Shaar 8, Ch. 3; Shaar 9, Ch. 2.</i> This is the root for the existence of the pleasures of this world.
Nevertheless, the principal aspect of evil is in the emotions, which branched far down into the husks (<i>Kelipah</i>) of <i>Asiyah.</i>
These are the wicked accusers who carry out actual evil, whose very [pleasure] in life is only to kill, like agents of death etc.
Below in this world, these are destructive creatures, such as snakes or predatory beasts etc., whereas in mankind these are the murderers.
Therefore, regarding the coming future when evil will be negated, it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">15</sup><i class="footnote">Isaiah 11:9 &amp; 65:25</i> “They will neither injure nor destroy [in all of My sacred mountain; for the earth will be filled with the knowledge of <i>HaShem</i>-יהו״ה as the water covers the ocean bed],” because then, the remnants of the seven kings [of <i>Tohu</i>], that have not yet been rectified, will have been purified, as known.
Now, in the “other side” of <i>Kelipah</i> there [also] is an aspect of the form of man. He is called, “Man without a yoke-<i>Adam Bleeya’al-</i>אדם בליעל,” and is the aspect of <i>Zeir Anpin</i> of <i>Kelipah</i>, like it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">16</sup><i class="footnote">Genesis 32:25; Shaar HaTeshuvah 49c</i> “And there wrestled a man with him etc.”
This is the aspect of the emotions with the intellect of <i>Abba</i> and <i>Imma</i> of the <i>Kelipah</i>-husks, including the aspect of <i>Keter</i> and <i>Atik Yomin</i> of <i>Kelipah,</i> which is called the depth of evil (<i>Omek Ra</i>),<sup class="footnote-marker">17</sup><i class="footnote">Sefer Yetzirah 1:5; Shaar HaTeshuvah Vol. 1, pg. 4a.</i> because it is the depth of the desire and pleasure for all wickedness, which is the source for all wicked desire.
In the Zohar these are called,<sup class="footnote-marker">18</sup><i class="footnote">Zohar III 41b; 70a;143a-b.</i> the “Crowns of Impurity - <i>Kitrin D'Mesavoota</i>” and in the terminology of the Talmud they are called,<sup class="footnote-marker">19</sup><i class="footnote">See also Shaar HaTeshuva Vol. 1, pg. 4b</i> “The gates of impurity etc.”
Now generally, there is the aspect of the ten <i>Sefirot</i> of <i>Kelipat Nogah</i> in [each world] of <i>Atzilut, Briyah</i>, <i>Yetzirah</i> and <i>Asiyah</i>.
However, in the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> there is no evil whatsoever, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">20</sup><i class="footnote">Psalms 5:5; Maamarei Admor HaZaken, Parshiot HaTorah Vol. 2, pg. 829; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch pg. 191.</i> “Evil shall not dwell with You etc.” Rather, it is the aspect of, “the sense of somethingness,” which is very pronounced and felt, such as the aspect of a person’s awareness of his own kindness, in that he glories in the kind deeds that he does.
Similarly, in regard to <i>Chochmah,</i> this is when he is very aware of his own wisdom. The same holds true of all one’s qualities and positive qualities. He knows and is aware of them in a very pronounced way.
What branches out as a result of this, leads to an aspect of actual evil. For example, in one who feels himself to be kind, there will branch out kindness that is only for his own self-aggrandizement and benefit, such as the kindness of Ishmael<sup class="footnote-marker">21</sup><i class="footnote">See Siddur Im Divrei Elokim Chayim, Shaar HaSukkot pg. 259c; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Na”Ch pg. 534.</i> and the like.
This then, is an example of the chaining down of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Briyah,</i> which branches out from <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Atzilut</i>, in that, all in all, it has a minority of evil,<sup class="footnote-marker">22</sup><i class="footnote">See the previous chapter.</i> which is the aspect of doing something for one’s own benefit, with the pride and haughtiness of a “something-<i>Yesh</i>,” separate and apart [from <i>HaShem</i>-יהו"ה] etc.
(For example, because of fervor during prayer, which is pronounced, in that he is aware of himself, a person will become angered against anyone who opposes him, to the point of striking and pursuing him, if his honor is slighted.)
Similarly, it states that,<sup class="footnote-marker">23</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Bava Batra 16a; See Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Vayikra Vol. 2, p. 476.</i> “Satan and Peninah’s intentions were for the sake of heaven” – which is the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Atzilut</i> – however, “he set his eyes on the first Temple and destroyed it.”<sup class="footnote-marker">24</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Sukkah 52a; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Bereshit pg. 98.</i>
This was from the aspect of the envy of the primordial snake,<sup class="footnote-marker">25</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Sanhedrin 59b; Maamarei Admor HaEmtzaee, Hanachot 5577, pg. 231; Torat Chayim, Bereishit 33a &amp; 16a.</i> [which is] the aspect of, “somethingness for the sake of oneself,” with a minority of evil, even though this envy came about because of his recognition and closeness, as [it states],<sup class="footnote-marker">26</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Avoda Zarah 55a</i> “Envy applies primarily [when the wise envies the wise, the mighty envies the mighty and the wealthy envies the wealthy] etc.”
<i>Nogah</i> of <i>Yetzirah</i> however, is half evil, with actual accusations, as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">27</sup><i class="footnote">Job 1:6 (2:1)</i> “And the Satan also came [amongst them] etc., and he said,<sup class="footnote-marker">28</sup><i class="footnote">Job 1:9</i> ‘does Iyov fear God without personal benefit etc.?’”
[It then descends further] until the aspect of <i>Nogah</i> of <i>Asiyah,</i> which is mostly evil, to actualize every harsh judgment, which literally is its vitality.
This is called,<sup class="footnote-marker">29</sup><i class="footnote">See Introduction to Zohar 11b.</i> “An evil whip with which to smite etc.” Moreover, it is like a leech that draws out the dross of the blood etc., as it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">30</sup><i class="footnote">Proverbs 30:15; Talmud Bavli, Avodah Zarah 17a</i> “The leech has [two daughters called] give, give etc.” This is the root of the aspect of hell (<i>Gehinom</i>) that will, “rest upon the heads of the wicked,”<sup class="footnote-marker">31</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Chagigah 13b</i> as known.
Now, the three impure <i>Kelipot</i>-husks are like the snake, serpent and scorpion in the, “desert of the nations.”<sup class="footnote-marker">32</sup><i class="footnote">Deuteronomy 8:15<i>; Likkutei Torah, Naso 20a; Shaar HaTeshuvah Vol. 1, p. 4b.</i></i>
[This is] the aspect of <i>Keter</i> of <i>Kelipah,</i> which is completely evil without any admixture of good whatsoever.
This is called<sup class="footnote-marker">33</sup><i class="footnote">Talmud Bavli, Brachot 7a; Tanya Ch. 11</i> a “<i>Rasha v'Ra Lo</i> - A wicked one who has bad,” for which as of yet, there is no rectification whatsoever, but rather, only in the future, about which it states,<sup class="footnote-marker">34</sup><i class="footnote">Zachariah 13:2</i> “I will – completely - remove the spirit of impurity” etc., as known. This will suffice for the understanding.
End of Shaar HaYichud
